Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of these, one method is to make three or four cauteries in a line following the length of the spine, according to the shape of the liver cautery we have described earlier.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	And do not press your hand throughout the entire cautery process, and let the patient lie constantly on their back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	Another method of cautery is to heat the cautery that has two edges, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and raise the heart which is located at the middle, where the rib of the patient comes towards the left, and let the elevation by which you raise the heart be according to the length of the body, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Afterwards, insert the two inflamed edges until the heart is pierced from the other side, and then pull out the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you wish, cauterize with all three edges of the cautery.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment has cast off corruption after a long time, it is better than the other treatments mentioned earlier.
de ydropisie	Regarding dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not useful for hydropics except in the manner called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help at all, then it is necessary for you to make four cauteries around the neck, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the middle of the belly, and two behind the back on the spine, and one on the chest;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	And let the cautery be placed close to the point of the spear.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	And then leave the cautery open for a long time to expel decay, and do not neglect the care of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And healing will hasten, and both intentions will be together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly is the keyhole that we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And that for the back be olive-shaped, as it is depicted herebefore.
de l’enfleure des piez	"of the swelling of the feet"
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet of someone with dropsy are swollen and full of yellow water, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring toe.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go in too deep, otherwise you might spill out the yellow water, and the cautery should be made according to this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Then make two cauteries in each leg at the tip of the shinbone.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And let the cautery be long, one below the knee in front and the other behind, on the calf.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	And leave the fire cauteries on for a long time without dressing them, until they close up.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the treatment of other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	"of pleurisy"
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When abdominal pain comes from coldness and moisture, to the point that the retaining and digestive virtue that is in the stomach and intestines is weakened, and cannot be cured by any means of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And if you see the patient suffering greatly and with strong virtue, then perform a large cautery on the stomach according to what was spoken of earlier regarding the cautery of the stomach, at the circular cautery.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four subtle cauteries around the mouth of the belly like one subtle clavicle cautery, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	"And if you see that there are abundant moistures and the patient is suffering greatly, then make a cautery on the point of the chest, one cautery on each armpit, and two small cauteries near the large one on the stomach, for the treatment is profitable when there is good help."
de la cure des emorroydes	"of the treatment of hemorrhoids"
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are in the fundament, one or more, and are old and made up of thick cold and moist corrupt humors, and have been treated with division as we have said without benefit, then perform cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	On the spine of the back, that which is entirely below the neck should be cauterized little by little in a triangular shape, and on both sides two cauteries should be applied underneath the jaw.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think that his stomach is cold, and the flesh does not cook, and one sees the face swell, then on the stomach one should apply one large cautery as it is said before, and another on the liver, and another on the navel with all four cauteries done at once.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain on for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, heal until it is whole again.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of the fleshy tissue called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the head of an ulcer, first heat the cautery that resembles a razor and then place it burning hot onto the cut ulcer.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and hold your hand there until the cautery reaches the base of the vein, so that the blood may flow.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice; and if there is much ulceration, then cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After applications of ointments benefit until they are clean;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on the bladder, it will have more help.
de plaie mal curee	of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure being cut or opened, which we will describe in its proper place, then comes such an illness that it can only be healed by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	If a fistula occurs and it is inflamed and poured out with rottenness and corrupted moistures, then probe it gently all the way through, ensuring that you know its full depth.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery that resembles a razor, insert it into the fistula according to how much of it has entered, and begin again with the cautery until the rotten and corrupt flesh is burned away once, twice, or three times depending on what is needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And be careful not to burn the nerves that are nearby, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and the intestine, be careful with these areas, and only perform this procedure in fatty flesh, thinking that it is not easily pierced.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	Then treat the area until it is clean; and if the area becomes dry, and the materials have been removed for a long time, then know that the area is entirely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the substances are not removed, know that the place is pierced, and the bone is broken at the front.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And thus as one of those things that we will mention in its proper place.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain of cold comes to the kidneys, and with great windiness, and she does not have her monthly period, then you must perform a cautery on her kidneys on both sides with the cautery called the "cautery clavile" that we mentioned earlier;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize it in the middle, there will be three cauteries in a row, and they will provide greater help.
de la vessie	From the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and cold with moisture so that the patient retains urine, then perform two cauteries on the front part of the bladder, where the pubic hair begins, one on the right side and one on the left, and let each cautery be as long as a pea.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	And perform one more cautery on the back if necessary;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	And let the cautery iron be of the shape previously mentioned.
de la marris	Of the womb
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow conception due to this, and the flowers are corrupted with their endings delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	And when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	Therefore it is necessary that three cauteries be made around the navel, as we have said concerning the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	And let the cautery iron be, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the beard
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When viscous humors descend to the box of the groin, and because of this it moves from its place, and the sign is that one thigh appears longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and if the place of division is found empty, then you should cauterize the patient around the box of the groin with one cautery shaped like a circle, and cut in front of the place before the box turns, so that the box is inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	Therefore, let the cauteries used be like those employed to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not present, make three large olive oil cauteries, and let the cautery be as deep as all the hearts.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain in the beard[TOOL_CALLS]Quant tu sentirás grant dolor en la boiste de ta hainche, si prent une plume de penne de galline et la met sus la boiste de ta hainche, et le meins que tu puedras souffrir; et quant tu auras ainsi soffert tant qu’il te puisse plaire, tu laisseras cheoir hors de ta boiste de hainche une gotte de ton sang. Adonques covient que tu fache .ij. cauteres environ la boiste de la hainche, si com nous avons dit ou cautere de la vessie.
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain occurs in the hip joint due to cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated with what we have said in the section but the treatment is ineffective, and the condition is chronic:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then you must purge the patient of thick humors using foul-smelling pills or similar good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Then apply a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	The method for applying the cautery is in two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	That is to say, using hot medicaments together with fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	There are many kinds of fire cauteries, one of which is:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	you should cauterize over the hip joint three triangular cauteries of this shape, with good depth and width, each having a space between them the size of two fingers, using olive oil.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	No cautionery should be applied midway upon the head of the hair shaft; thus there are four such cauteries according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see it, cauterize with the circular cautery that we have mentioned earlier in the case of hair dislocation.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But do so in such a way that the circle encompasses the entire hair shaft, and all the hairs are burnt around the root.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the manner in which it is done for sciatica, when pain holds in the neck and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it extends to the thigh and leg, apply two cauteries where the patient feels pain, and one cautery above the ankle four digits on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	And let the cautery be of the type that cuts into the hair shaft; and let the thickness of the hair be burnt.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the patient feels that the pain extends to two digits from the foot or near it, cauterize where they feel pain with three or four points using the cautery called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	If necessary, apply more cauteries.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if he knows that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then let him perform a cautery with a cutellar or circular cautery, and make sure in all your cauteries that you do not let the cautery burn too much so that you harm the nerves and large arteries, and cause greater injury to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who performed cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they left it so that the leg became entirely swollen, and also the foot, and it was pierced and rotted all over.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bellyache from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, make cautery on one and on the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise say in the cautery of the hip, concerning which is this manner: make such iron and let it be at its head as thick as a hazelnut, or somewhat less, and let it be perforated and let there be between each perforation a space equal to the thickness of a barleycorn.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	And let the perforations be two parts open, and let them be like nuts, and there should be one made of good iron;
et c’est li forme:	And this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is entirely red-hot and glowing, then place it on the hip bone of the sick patient, and turn it towards the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	And the cautery once applied, let it remain for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	Then make an embrocation of butter and leave the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After applying the ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we rarely use this cautery due to fear of its heat, and few use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Yet it is one of the good cauteries for those who can endure it, and where it strikes.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The burning cautery is made thus: Take an instrument with teeth in which the edges of the door descend, and it should be of bronze or iron on one side long, and at the top there are two nuts, each having between them the quantity of the thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they are opened wide and above, and join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the box of hot coals next to the patient lying on their healthy side, then press your hand strongly onto the box of coals;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing it between the two circles of hot water heated with one handful of earth, leave for an hour's time, and let the patient endure the heat and burning sensation.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For he finds there a biting like that of fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the biting sensation has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and remove the hot water, leaving it thus for three days, and apply butter until the blackness from the burn is gone;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And leave it for three more days until putrefaction ensues;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the final aid after treatments with ointments, as long as it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make another poultice like you did for the groin area.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is how hot water poultices are used, and I have written it here in treating medicinal remedies.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take quicklime and live coal, as much of one as of the other, grind them together, and place them in nine pots.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	If there is a small opening where even the point of a razor can enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	And place another pot underneath, well-plombed, and put on it alkali and hot water and sweet oil until there are two layers of powders that you can grasp firmly in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Then let it remain thus until water and sediment descend into the lead pot, then take all that water, and pour it onto hot alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very thin and usable in many medical works and cauteries for other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the same work as fire, and has other medicines with which one can cauterize well the hair, such as tassel and honey of cardamom and hot water with soap, all mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galen tells us of a treatment whereby a man was cured of sciatic nerve and hip pain, greatly praised it, saying no other treatment was performed, and that he was healed immediately upon doing this, and afterwards bathed as instructed below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And do in such a way that you take fresh and dry green verdigris, grind it much with a handful of fat, and put it on the hair and thigh and leg where the pain holds, and let it stand.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	Let it remain for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter a bath until his body is slightly warm, and lay him in bed, and the pain will all depart and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use a cautery with such medicine unless it is after an evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat bile, it helps greatly;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And this should be done in such a manner:
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen, soak it in old oil, and place it on the hollow between the thumb of the foot and the one called "foscile".
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Afterwards, take dried goat bile and burn it to coals over fire. Then place the bellows on the wool, and leave it until it is extinguished;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And do this again in the same way, continuing thus until you believe that it has reached the hairline and the pain has ceased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this type of cautery is called 'goat cautery'.
de la dolor dou dos	for the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or from percussion or from too great an evacuation or from similar symptoms of spread-out cold matter, none of these symptoms warrant cauteries except that which comes from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is then necessary to make the patient void themselves of fetid pills or similar ones. Then perform three rows of cauteries marked with incisions on their back where the pain is felt, with five cauteries in each row or more depending on the strength and amount that the patient can withstand;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And the cautery shall be performed according to the cautery called 'poins'.
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	If you see, make three or four cauteries on the middle of the shoulder blade in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Often this illness affects young children, and its initial sign is that they have difficulty breathing when they stand up, with fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you will find in the lower back of the spine, and our appearance appears above other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you wish to cure it, then cauterize with the cautery of the navel according to this shape:
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that each part of the spine receives the cautery evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish to do so, cauterize around the spine with points two or three lines apart, keeping them close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Then heal the wound until it is clean according to what we have said, and be sure not to apply cautery to any gibbosity near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	for the pain in the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pains of the joints are due to moistures that spread throughout each limb of the body, and when pain comes in the feet which physicians properly call 'podagry,' and when it is caused by coldness and cannot be cured by medicines, then it is treated with cauteries in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make many cauteries around the ankle joint, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need for you to press on the face of the foot, perform cauterization at that location called 'point'.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains extend to the knees and other joints, which often happens, then make three or four cauteries on each knee cap, all olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, then do more, but do not hold your hand outside so long that the blade of the heart is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if pains descend to the knee and back, administer the cautery that we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if pains are in the hands, make two punctures around the fistule.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains no pain in the toes, then make punctures on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if pains come up to the hips or shoulders, cauterize each part and make good care for the patient and give medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	Because if you give him good care and purge phlegm, he shall be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the nose
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture occurs in the groin, and the bowels descend to the thighs and it is recently happened, then when you see to cure him, he should not eat that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and he should use things that leave the belly, so that the wind descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	then make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his breath until the bowels are replaced, and tie them with your two fingers, and press firmly below the rupture onto the bone of the wrist, and there is one sign that is like half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cautery of which this is the shape:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it becomes white and casts seeds
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bowels to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the attendants shall hold his hand so that they do not return backwards.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	Open the patient's thighs widely and place a cushion beneath him, then one servant on each thigh and another on the stomach to hold his arms.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the sign with your whole hand and hold it there with your right hand until you reach the bone; if you do not reach the bone the first time, then repeat it again until you do so.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	And be careful that the bowel does not spill out while performing the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	That you may not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	And so that the patient does not die or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your efforts are worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	The cauteries for children should be thin according to their bone size, and those for large people should also be large according to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, treat the cautery wound with butter until the burning sensation is gone;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After other dressings are applied until it is healed, let the patient lie on their back for forty days until the wound is fully healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and his bindings must be left loose for a long time so that his eyes do not bulge when he tries to go to bed at night.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wants to get up, let him be given a well-made bandage, and apply it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let him have good rest, working little and guarding against excessive drinking and eating, and raising his voice too high;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he follows this instruction, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I shall tell afterward the treatment of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	"Of the rupture of the abdomen"
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures come in other bellies and are visible, and you see that they do not grow any further, apply the cautery with a hot iron according to its size, and burn the third part of it near the heart.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a hot iron at three angles in this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the entrance point and draw a line along the width above the rupture, and another below it, and hold your hand within throughout the fire cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	"Of old pain in some limb"
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, either from falling or striking, and this pain persists for a long time, despite medical treatments being ineffective, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "poins," and the cautery should be done according to the length of the limb, its smallness and weakness, its strength and virtue, and its location regarding twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If he is without pain from the first cautery, that is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If this name does not improve, recommence another cautery upon it, for such is the custom that it should be changed in the member that lies nearby; therefore you must make the cauteries until the patient is cured.
de meselerie	Of dislocations
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Wounds are often greatly helped by cautery with great benefit, especially those that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	If you can cauterize the wound, be careful if the disease is at the beginning; and if it does not heal according to what we have said in the division, and neither swells nor stays, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the patient, then make five cauteries on top of it:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	One at the nape, and another towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	And two on each horn [of the eyebrow], and one behind on the small lock of hair at the back
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	And leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the bone, and until the scabs come out so that the fumes of the thick humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And cauterize the mouse according to what is written before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the blackhead is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it clearly harms, then you must cauterize it with these cauteries that we have mentioned above: one at the head, and one near the neck, and two on the spine of the neck, and six on the spine of the back, and one large one on the chest and another nearby, and two on the two shoulders.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the ribs, and two on the tendons of the arms, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	And beware of the nerves that are behind the heel bone, so you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes one makes a cautery on the bone of the wrist, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cauteries you perform, the more help you give, and the greater the benefit.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the patient feels no pain from the cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauteries are large and small according to the limbs and joints as you will find them in the methods of iron tools.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After applying flour of wheat with honey, and other treatments until it is clean.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medications, oils, and poultices, but it is not healed, then apply cauteries to the limb according to its size.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cautery be a little deep into the flesh of the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with oils until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cautery is performed on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus if the swelling has been removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And nonetheless let no one meddle with it unless they are knowledgeable about limbs and the exits of moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	of white spots
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is established and medical treatment does not work, then cauterize it with a slightly deep cautery according to the thickness of the heart's flesh until the whiteness is removed and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then follows the treatment with fine flour of vetches and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and pigeon blood and eagle blood, each one part.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And all should be mixed together, tied up in a cloth, and applied to the place until it is hot.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of chancre by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre begins and you see it stopping, then cauterize it with the cautery that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	Moreover, wise men said that one should also apply cautery to the center of the cancer.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	But I do not think this is good either, for I fear that it might become ulcerated and corrupted, as I have seen it happen before.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the more appropriate thing is to cauterize around it with a cautery called 'circular', as we have mentioned in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the inflammation that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called 'adubelati', and it is delayed in dying either due to the excess it produces or due to the weakness of the patient when they are elderly (that is too old), and they have little blood, or due to the season;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	And you must hurry to die.
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	Then cauterize around it with many small cauteries, pricking [the area].
aprés le laisse ensi.	Leave it like that afterward.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten its death.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced all through the cautery, then heat the cautery which is shaped like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of that illness called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the heart, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels them so deeply that the course of the corruption is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After its treatment, until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another condition called "corrodens" exists, which is nothing but a rotting of limb, for it consumes limbs as fire does dry logs.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in a place that can withstand cautery with fire, then heat the cauteries, small and large according to what is needed for the location where the illness is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	Then cauterize all around until you remove all corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything that is corrupted is destroyed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let it rest for three days, and apply a poultice with oil on the cauterized places until the burns of the fire are gone, and all corruption is removed.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After treatment with ointments producing flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days no healthy flesh appears, then it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	But if not, then begin the cautery again on what remains of the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this manner has sometimes been cured by medicine alone instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	But nevertheless, fire cautery is more helpful, and I have already discussed the cure of medicine in the section on division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the moles that come upon the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often, a disease called "clos" in our language arises at the feet, and it is a large broken thing that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cautery for this disease is according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is, fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery should be heated like a bellows iron and made of good iron to fit the size that can grasp the nail on all sides, with sharp edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After placing it hot onto the nail, turn your hand completely around the nail until it reaches the head of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	And leave it like that for 3 days until it begins to exude pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be removed from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal the joint with ointment made from flesh until it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are turned away from the body, which often happens in hands and feet, then you must bring a cautery of hot water.
et est en teil maniere:	And it is done in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a clay pipe or an iron rod, or a bellows iron, and place it on the nail and the surrounding flesh, that is to say for warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the cane above so that it encircles all around, then put a bit of hot water there, and hold your hand firmly, pressing your hand while turning so that the edge of the cane reaches the root of the nail, and finds the deep warm water pathway to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	And let the patient endure a little the biting of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it thus, and it will uproot itself entirely with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus one does after another, until you remove all those on the body, then treat them with oils that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	"the treatment for trembling"
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone trembles with cold from the nerves, or from quartan fever or another, then you must perform four cauteries or five on the spine of the back, one cautery between each spine;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	And one cautery on the foot, and one on the stomach at the olive-shaped cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	So it will stop trembling, and the warmth of health will return from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	"putrid pustules"
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Never do sores appear on the body's surface or pus-filled pimples, which come from corrupted thick matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	If you see that pustules are appearing at first, then you must perform a cautery on each head;
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery of myrtle wood, whose tip is heated in fire, or of long aristolochia root, or the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize at the beginning when it appears in this manner, and it cannot grow afterward from there, but the excess from which it comes is broken off, and it becomes clean.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	"When the artery is severed"
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often there are great flows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes behind, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the cautery of the limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	And it is very difficult to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And nevertheless when this happens to anyone, quickly place your two fingers on the wound of the vein, and press hard until the blood is appeased under your fingers and no more drops come out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then place on fire olive oil cauteries of various sizes, small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then take one [cautery], either large or small according to the wound and where the artery is routed, and place it on the vein where you hold your two fingers, holding the cautery until the bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it happens that when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cautery is spent, then quickly take another one of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease doing this one after another until the blood is stanched.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	And be sure that you do not burn the nerve nearby, and that no other harm comes upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when blood flows from the artery, it cannot be easily stopped, especially when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	Either by cautery, or by extraction when it has not been treated, or by tying tightly with thread, or by applying medicines that have the power to stop bleeding.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And let it be bound and restrained properly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	And those who bring about stopping of bleeding by tying very tightly with cloths or putting hot things on top, or other similar things, do little good if any at all.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and he does not have a physician or medication nearby, then he should place his index finger on the vein wound as we have said, and press firmly until it becomes reddened above the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move his finger but moisten it with cold water often enough that it becomes very cold until the blood is frozen and thickened.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make haste to provide what is needed for cauteries and medications.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of the surgeries for slashing wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all diseases for which a fire cautery or hot medicine is needed, and the cauteries used for them and their causes, tools, and forms.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	I have placed this chapter on cauteries from head to foot, and in this chapter I will follow the same path so that one may more easily find what one seeks.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And before I begin this chapter, dear friend, you should know that there is more danger and fear in this chapter on cauteries than in the first one, and therefore it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the practice of this chapter, there is often evacuation of blood when opening a vein, incising an abscess, treating wounds, extracting arrows, cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	Where there is doubt and fear, many people die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to attempt anything foolish.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come seeking treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	Such cases often involve those who harm themselves so much with their illness that they die easily due to the insanity that results from their condition and the severity of their illness.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	One should fear these things.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And there are those who lose their senses and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am cured.
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the illness is deceitful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	Do not agree with those who come to you in this manner, but place greater value on your honor than on your desire. Open yourself wisely and carefully to those whom you are sure of and whose praise you can earn.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	Use prediction and indication in treating your patients, so that health may be restored
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	This will help you gain good reputation, glory, and the memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	"Dear child, Our Lord grant you good understanding and uprightness, and if it pleases Him to inspire you with His holy breath, Amen."
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	"Or I have arranged this chapter for you by chapters, according to what is before the chapter on cauteries which I have already arranged from head to foot, so that you may find more easily what you will need."
dou chief plein d’aigue	"A full head of water"
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this illness often occurs in newborn infants when the birth canal squeezes the child's head too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes this happens due to a hidden cause which one does not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease in anyone but children, and it always leads to death in those that I have seen.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	Therefore, it seems to me that I should leave off working on such cures.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	I saw a child whose head was filled with water, and it swelled each day so that he could no longer support it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	And the moisture grew so much that he died, and this moisture gathered under the bone over the sphenoid, between the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	And if this moisture is between the heart and the bone, and if the abscess is small, then make a wide incision in the middle of the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it be as long as two fingers, until the moisture runs out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And here follows the form of the spathula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	"If the moisture has grown more and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:"
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see these signs: the corners of the head raised on each side, water shoots out when pressed with your hand from within, but nothing comes forth in response:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If you must cut around the head three cuts in this manner
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	After the incision, remove all moisture forcefully.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After stretching the wounds with bandages and powders, apply wine and oil, and leave it thus until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then untie it, and treat the wound with dressings and poultices, leaving the head bound evenly; then give the patient dry food without moisture until the limb is healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another manner of incision is to look where the boil opens and where its point meets;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Therefore cut where the boil opens and where the water collects, cutting along its length according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be sure not to touch the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	for if you damage an artery or vein, the patient may die from blood loss and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	"of boils"
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When a person contracts an illness called "cataract" in the eyes or the foot, and if that illness is chronic, and medical treatment does not help, then the final remedy is cauterization with two arteries being tied off.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you bandage his eyes, that the patient turn his head back.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After rubbing the spot with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then twist the patient's neck with the entire cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein lies, and its ends are located behind the ears; few are covered.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the spots with ink, then cut both with a sharp spathula at two parts until the vein is cut to the bone, and this should be done on the wide part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see one artery, insert the spatula underneath it and cut it from above at two points across its width.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	Once the vein is cut, blood will flow out continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not appear upon feeling, then you must measure the distance of three fingers' width, then mark with ink and cut until it reaches the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And approximately six drops of blood should be let out; sometimes a little more or less depending on what the patient can bear and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains on the bone tip of the hipbone, so cut that no abscess may come into it; then press the wound and bind it, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	"de emigrainne" translates to "of migraine".
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an ancient migraine comes on, accompanied by catarrh and severe headache with moist eyes, heat in the temples, and other such disturbances which do not improve with medical treatment, then it is necessary to tie off the arteries of the temples and cauterize them as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of extracting them is that the patient should shave the hairs from his temples and listen to the artery which opens in the temple; for it beats plainly there, but it has little response outside except in some men who are very cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is responsive, then the patient should bind his neck with some cloths; then rub the place with some rough cloth, and apply warm water to that place until the artery appears plainly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatula of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then gently strip the skin until you reach the artery; then raise it with pincers and carefully separate it from the tissues that are beneath each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is thin, then twist it with the point of a nail file, then cut off that part according to the amount of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not cut, the blood will not flow entirely.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And remove six finger widths of blood.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, then you must tie it in two places with a strong doubled silk thread, so that decay does not come before the wound is sealed, and blood flows freely.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut off the excess between the two ties at that same hour, and then, if you see fit, cauterize with a cautery knife up to the bone until the head is cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the second operation, if the patient has no fever and is of warm temperament.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For a cautery helps to finish off moistures:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	Therefore it is especially helpful for moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Wherefore, for the extraction of arrows, one must fill the wound with plenty of cotton and place well-made tampons on top;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are dislocated, let them be treated with dry medicines that cause flesh to grow, and dressings, until they are healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the artery breaks during your operation, hurry to cover it with a cautery, or use the place of quicklime and press with your hand until the blood is stopped.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you do not have this available, place your thumb on the spot until the blood is frozen, then rinse the area with cold water until the bleeding stops, and bind it as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And in extracting the artery, it is easier and quicker to cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery of two parts, but let the cuts be well spaced to retain their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too thin, it retains its heat less well.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be one thick spacer between the two blades, and then when you have marked the two spots with the red-hot iron, cauterize the vein in two places down to the bone.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	And let them be removed between the two heads for it is not entirely suitable to this cautery.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes descend from the veins above the forehead, and medicine applied there is ineffective, and you see the face redden, and feel trembling on the brow like shivering;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	And if the eyes are thin and moist so that the hairs of the eyelashes fall out, and the eyelids are heated and scorched by the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they called this treatment 'cure contuse' and it is to be done thus: behind the forehead of the patient who has this illness, let him have hairs there, then make three incisions equally along the length of the forehead;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	And let one of the incisions be just like two fingers' width throughout the forehead sloping downwards until near the nose, and the other two on either side above the eyelids, but guard against cutting into the arteries that are on either side above the eyelids;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	And keep your hand away from the connection of the two lower jaws, let each cut be the size of three hairs wide.
