puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat those with appropriate ointments until they are healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	And if the abscess is due to the incision of a vein, then you should cut around the entire skin of the abscess with your hand, then place the needle beneath the spot you are holding and pierce it until there is one doubled thread that can be pulled from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then tie off the abscess, as I have told you, with the ligament of one of two parts using the thread.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you doubt that the thread is not hot enough, then insert another needle alongside all the threads below the entire abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tie the threads in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut away the abscess until the surplus comes out; then cut away the surplus from the heart and leave what is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put a cloth dampened in wine and oil on it; then apply dressings and poultices until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	"Boils on the nerves"
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	"So boils can also occur on nerves when they are struck or from too much physical exertion and similar causes."
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens most often at shoulders and hips, and in all places where there are joints; it is a serious abscess, its color resembles the color of flesh, and it occurs in many ways without pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when it is pressed strongly, the patient feels pain, but it is not deep within the body, rather below the heart.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And it moves well in all directions, and does not go forward or backward, down or up; those that are in joints should not be cut with a knife:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	It might happen that there would be contraction there.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And he who is at the head or forehead, cuts the skin with a scalpel.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, grasp it with tongs and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it is large, suspend it with forceps and scrape it, then remove the bone and sew the wound closed, caring for it until it is healed.
des grosses boces pendans	"hanging pouches"
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes this occurs in bellies and nowhere else, and it is a disease called "funge" due to its resemblance; it has thin roots and large heads.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	And among them there are some small ones and many very large ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	I have seen someone who had two in the belly that were more like fungi than anything else; they were white, had fine roots, and were often split open, with moisture always flowing from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them out and found one weighing 18 ounces and the other 6; upon opening them, it was evident that the patient was moist, with the flesh appearing pale, moist, and having fine roots.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	If he strikes the shoulder blade widely, and if there are cauteries with fire before you.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For in cutting, it often happens that too much blood flows out, and if the blood gushes forth, then hasten to cauterize.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	And if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the cut by iron, then take a well-made string of lead, and tie the artery as we have said, leaving it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	And then bind it, and do not cease twisting the string of lead until you strike the artery, and cut through it without labor.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	And if the roots are large, then one fears cutting even for the belly, but you can indeed cut half of it, then cauterize so that it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and make sure you do not cut the lobe which is of fox-like color, poor sense, and produces milk.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an enchanted aposteme, and I will come to the cure of cancer hereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	When the boil has burst
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If swelling appears due to cautery of a wound or incision from syphilis, and it is on the belly and in some cases among the bowels, as happens with other sores, or from blood issuing from veins or arteries according to what is before
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it's due to the rupture of the spleen and the exit of bile, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the body, and it is a light thing without pain, and there are various exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is for the outlet of the intestines, then it is more diverse. And when you press it with your fingers, it rises up and then returns. And sometimes it is seized, and greatly enlarged at the entrance of the anus and by violent effort.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it's due to moisture, it's a light thing, and opens well when you press it with your hand, without constraining.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if it's due to blood, then the abscesses open with these signs: large and hard, and are stuck according to a certain quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it's due to windiness, then it is soft to the touch, and the work is such that you look to see if the appearance is for arterial blood, or venous blood, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	It is necessary that you leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, concerning the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is for the intestines or the bladder, then you must command the patient to stain their armpit and stretch it out straight, then press all around the belly.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then command them to lie still between your hands, then go around the place that you have marked with all the spatula, then stretch half of the abscess upwards with the whole large finger.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then wrap it around with a strong thread or silk cord tightly, and let it remain so.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then open half of the boil over the ligature, and insert your index finger into it to search for the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find it caught in the ligature, untie it, and bring the intestine out of the abdomen;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the boil, grasp it with forceps and cut off its excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	If the artery or vein opposes you, go around it carefully, then return to your work and take two needles, thread two strong threads through them, and insert the two needles around what you have done in a cross-stitch pattern;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then press the boil in four places over the needles, and if you see fit, remove the needles, leaving them there until it rots, and cut away the dead flesh.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	And when it becomes subtle and rotten, cut it off there, then treat what is necessary, and cauterize the boil as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	Extract the blood or moisture that you find,
dou chancre	chancre
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have spoken of the likenesses of chancre in the division [of this book], and how one ought to operate by means of medicines there, and how one should avoid the cure with iron.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we say the chancre that invades the marrow, and great caution in its treatment. The ancients said that when chancres are located where they can be shaved, such as those on breasts, hips, and similar areas, one should remove them entirely at the onset.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	And when it is large and old, do not attempt to approach it, for I have never seen any healed in such cases.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	Never has anyone been cured of it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And when the operation is in a location where it can be removed, as we have said, you should purge the patient of black bile once.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then make him fast if he shows signs of repletion, then place the patient in a good location to perform the operation.
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	Then pour on your ointments around the cancer, and shave all the hair off, and scrape away everything without leaving anything.
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And let the blood flow freely, and press well on the spot with your hand or any object; if the bleeding from the incision of the artery or vein troubles you, cauterize it until the blood stops.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with other treatments until it is healed.
de ydropisie	Regarding dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already discussed in the section on dropsy its similarities, how water collects in it, and the signs of each type, and treatment by medications, and that treated by iron.
si est eclites soulement;	So is this one specifically mentioned.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	And in these two types, one should not touch them with iron:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	Namely, tympanites and hydrocele, for they are deadly.
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when treating this type of dropsy called 'eclipses' with medications and the treatment does not help, look to see if the patient is weak or has another disease besides dropsy, such as coughing, diarrhea, etc.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	If you do not touch iron to it, there is doubt [about its effectiveness].
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	And if you see the patient with strong vitality, and they have no other illness but dropsy alone, and are not too young nor too old, then you should proceed thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Lift the patient upright onto your hands, and have the assistants press the abdomen using water at its lowest part, then take the spine in this manner:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be sharpened at both ends.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	At an angle, but not so deep that it can reach the intestines when inserted, and not sharp enough to wound;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	Then observe whether the dropsy has entered towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	If so, you must make three incisions directly below the navel using a knife;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	And if the dropsy is due to liver disease, then make your incision to the left of the navel.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	And if it is due to worms, then make your incision on the right side, and ensure that the patient does not lie directly above where the incisions are made so that excess fluids do not drain into this weak area.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	Then pierce all the hide with the instrument and insert it; raise your hand entirely over the spatula between the hide and the skin as in flaying, to the quantity of one nail or even more around.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Then pierce the skin until the spatula reaches its proper place; this is where the water emerges. Then heat this instrument and insert it as follows:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it resembles a thin silver tube, made of brass or light iron, with a small hole at one end.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	And on one side, three holes
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	And two on the other side, and one on the other
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	And the head is cut like a feather, this is the shape of the incision with which writers trim their feathers
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	At the top above is the funnel, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it should now be placed over it.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	Empty it then of half or a third part; for if you empty more than is necessary at that time, the patient may perhaps die from the dissolution of his spirit by the weapon, or fall into a swoon, or approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	But pour out according to its quantity of power, and according to what the dispositions of the patient's virtue signify, and his breath.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	Then draw the instrument and hold the water, which is now retained by the heart blocking the opening that is above the stomach, as I have spoken about, piercing according to this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	Then recommence the instrument on another day if you see the patient enduring these things, and draw out a small quantity of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	Do this for several days, but be careful not to draw too much so that only a little bit of water remains.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and leave much water in him, then treat it with hot salt or sand, and often wash him with sweat or baths and sun exposure, and apply ointments to drink.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And treat with drying medications until he is healthy, and cauterize on the stomach and liver and spleen after extracting the water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	"Regarding the obstruction of the instrument"
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without any opening in their penis, or with a small opening, or one that is not in the correct place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If it needs to be done immediately, pierce it with a very fine spatula according to this shape:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then place over the hole this thin tin covering, and secure it, holding it thus for three or four days. When he wishes to urinate, remove the cover, let him do so, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And perhaps there is no need for this, as the hot urine will not leave through the closed area.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose wound is small, let him apply clay of lead, as we have said; it will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the opening in its proper place are handicapped, for some are born with the opening at the end of the penis, which prevents them from urinating unless they raise their penis upwards.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	They also cannot ejaculate because the matter cannot reach the mouth of the urethra, and this is a serious condition.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the manner of performing this operation is that the patient lies on his back. Then stretch out the head of the penis and bind it tightly like the shaft of a feather, so that the opening falls in the middle, as it should.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And beware of bleeding that often occurs there, and if it does happen, stop it with whatever stops bleeding, and heal the wound until it is clean.
des pustules de la verge	"Regarding the pustules of the penis:"
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times these blisters come upon the penis, appearing as ugly flesh.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	And among them are malicious ones and non-malicious ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	Therefore, you should prick them with a fine needle, cut and cleanse all of them, then place moistened cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment upon them;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with diaphoretic ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the wound is malignant, foul-colored and foul-smelling, then you must apply cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it open and if the blister is on top of the penis with some part inside the foreskin and some outside, then you must first remove the blister that is inside;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And once it's removed, then treat what remains outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For if you treat them together, the head of the penis may be pierced, and blackness and corruption come to its tip and its opening.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore cut away all that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster made of honey and flour mixed with the peel of pomegranates and figs, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding starts, then apply the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauteries help with two conditions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	That is to say, for the removal of blood, and for gangrene;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, you must insert a lead tube into the penis, and the patient will urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the foreskin at the head of the penis is stuck, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or due to wound or abscess, then you must cauterize it with a hot iron until the bonds are released and the glans of the penis is freed from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if it is difficult to separate them, then you must cauterize with the spéculum some of the head of the penis and foreskin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then gently pull apart both sides, and place a thin linen cloth soaked in cold water between them so that it does not stick again.
de la circoncision	"Regarding circumcision:"
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Nevertheless when we perform this work of our will, especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best and easiest work for their health.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	"I say that the ancients did not mention the circumcision of their children because they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experience."
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For most masters and surgeons performing circumcision use irons, forceps, and an entire novacula
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	But if the heart fails because there are two layers, sometimes one is cut above and the other remains below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Otherwise, it should be cut again, causing double pain, and during healing, the tip of the member may not be securely attached.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And during healing of the nail, sometimes the iron slips, spoiling the work; many times they are born this way and do not require healing.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	"Regarding the cleansing that is done with forceps along the entire length of the thread, I have found through experience that it is good because forceps cut equally well above and below."
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, cut evenly in one second.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	But make sure the thread is tightly wrapped around the skin
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	And the manner of the first work should be that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the penis and not harming him in any other way
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	Then make it stay between your hands straight, and hide the tools under your feet so that the child does not see them nor any of the instruments.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then place your hand on the neck and blow near the heart, and pull up until the head of the neck is inside;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the wound closed with a doubled thread, then tie below the pouch to the other string
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it there with the second ligature on the pouch and the index finger, and cut between the two strings, then raise the heart quickly and pull the head of the neck
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow pouch and pouch, for that is the medicine;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and sprinkle powder on it and over the powder apply a cloth dipped in cooked egg yolk tempered with rosewater, mixed with good fresh rosemary oil, and leave it there until the next day, then treat again until healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the cauterization for purification is thus:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Both heads [of the cautery] should be thin and sharp-pointed, and let them be as long as a finger evenly.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The mistake in cauterization is when the heart is inside the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you must stretch it to your fingernail before the boil appears;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And cut evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your finger, then use forceps, and then cut.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it lasts for three days, and what is under the shaft is swollen, then leave it until the boil calms down, and gently scrape off the scab;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	Then cut as much as you can move, but be careful not to harm the part of the shaft, for it will do no harm.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Therefore, treat the place with sudden wound powder, which we have discussed in treating powders; and if you cut too much of the heart, it will not be harmed.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Heal it then, as we have said, until it is healthy.
dou retenement de l’urine	"On the retention of urine"
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to obstruction from a stone, or coagulated blood, or bowel, or flesh born, or similar things, as we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if urine is not released and you see that it is retained because of a stone lodged in the neck or bladder, then the patient must be bent forward on his knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And let him put his feet on his back, and extend his belly from the part above the back, and let the patient hold himself up as much as he can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And then the neck of the bladder is forced open for the expulsion of the stone above, whereupon the urine will be released.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come out as we have said and the patient feels great pain, then you must use all instruments called "syngenes" for extraction.
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And let there be a light, subtle silver chain, like the feather of a bird.
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And let the chain be one and a half palms long, and thin at its end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the manner of the issue of urine is that you take a doubled thread, tie at its head a pouch of wool or cotton, and put the head of the thread inside the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And cut off the excess wool and put it up to the head of the syringe; then grease the syringe with oil or butter mixed with egg yolk, and make the patient sit on a seat, and raise his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently insert the syringe into the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis; then fold the penis upwards towards the belly.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder; the patient will feel it when it is empty. But if this is not done correctly, it may be because the tube leading to it is twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then they pull the thread all over the wool bit by bit, and the urine follows the wool; then pull out the thread, and make the urine run.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and continue squeezing the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	Here are some examples of what "des maladies de la vessie" might mean in English:
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When the skin is peeled off and blood flows into the bladder, or putrefaction has gathered there, and you see that water and medications are being distilled from it, then use all the instruments called "clepsydra," and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	II on one side, and I on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the raised places where the medicine is applied should fit tightly around the penis so that it can be drawn closed without additional help to keep out moisture when needed.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicine entering the bladder, place the head of the funnel in the moisture and draw up what is inside it
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	and then tightly plug the funnel.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	Then the moisture will enter and reach the bladder, causing the patient to feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	And this is the form of the subtle enema used for bladder enemas
si est ci:	Here is:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And is made of silver or lead, and the head is higher.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and below it leans on the chest where the links fall;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with the moisture you want to use for sitz baths; then tie it between both breasts with a good doubled thread and heat this moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then place the mouth of the sitz bath in the rectum, then press your hand on the bladder until all the moisture has flowed into the bladder, so that the patient feels it has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment and make a circle from it and pierce it evenly around the edges;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread into these holes; then gather the circle together like a sieve and put inside it whatever oil, moisture, and water you wish, and tie it to the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, pressing your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	"de la pierre"
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have previously mentioned in the division the types of stone and their removal along with medicines.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And I have said the difference between a stone that enters the bladder and all its signs, and in which stone one should operate by cutting.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that stones which enter the bladder often happen in children, and it is a sign that water leaps from the bladder like water in its fineness;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and it is apparent when hair appears, and grit is felt by the patient's penis, and he urinates many times and then becomes constipated.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	And often these are the fundamentals;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the cure of children is easy until they reach four years old, and it is very difficult in old men, and it is medium for those between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the cure is easier for those who have a large stone than for those who have a small one.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with a clyster, to draw out all the filth that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes obstructs seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then seize the patient by the feet, tip him over and move him downward so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and ejects sometimes from the high place;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have him sit between your hands prepared, and his hands beneath his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then locate it and touch it inside
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in the space, then now hasten to cut upon the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall upon touching it all over, then moisten your left index finger with oil if the patient is a child, or your middle finger if the patient is an adult man.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into its base, and seek out the stone; when you feel it with your finger, then move it towards the neck of the bladder
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press upon your finger and expel it there where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press upon the bladder with his hand; and command him to extend his right hand upwards with the scrotum, and with his left hand remove the skin that is beneath the scrotum in the part where you will make the cut
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then pour in the spatumic acid, of which this is the formula:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between what is between the thighs and the fundament, not in the middle but on the left side toward the navel;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And let it be straight upon the stone, and your two hands always on the fundament; and make the incision across so that it is wide at its entrance but narrow within, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	In case the pressure causes the hand on the fundament to slip without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	And know that there are stones with corners and edges.
si est griés a issir;	If it is difficult to pass out;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And some are smooth like a glass marble, and round, whose exit is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those with corners and edges, make the incision larger.
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	And if it does not come out, then you must use tongs like a chisel's head to grasp and remove the stone so that it does not escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	When you place beneath the inflamed instrument its curved head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	And if you cannot manage it thus, then widen the little hole a bit, and if blood flows out, constrain it with powdered glass.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And if there are more than one stone, then insert the largest first at the neck of the bladder, then cut it open, then remove the thread, and afterwards remove the smaller ones if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be so, and a larger wound must be made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or urine flows continuously from a place where flesh cannot heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	But nevertheless try to remove it using forceps or cutters until you remove it piece by piece.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And when you have completed your task, then fill the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and constrain it, and place upon it a moistened cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then raise the patient's head, and do not untie the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And when you untie it, then wash the area very well with oil and water, then dress it with diapheconointment and basilicon ointment until it is healed."
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if an abscess occurs in the wound with corrosions and clots of blood in the bladder, causing retention of urine in this manner that it cannot pass without effort with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Therefore, apply a poultice to the wound and remove that blood, for if it remains, it will harm the bladder and corrupt it.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then wash the wound with water and honey and salt, and help him in all ways that you know until he is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that every time you treat him, you bind his two thighs together and apply the medicine to its proper place.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis and stuck within, and urine cannot pass out:
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	Then perform the treatment that I have mentioned earlier, cutting it many times until it is relieved from the cutting; otherwise, excuse yourself from this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already tested it thus.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	"Take one iron rod according to this shape and let it be forked at three ends stuck into one stick:"
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take some thread and wind it around the stalk below the stone so that it cannot move backwards into the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then insert the drill gently into the stalk until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and slowly twist the drill by hand against the stone little by little until you can pierce the stone from the other side
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	When urine begins to flow, then press your hand on what remains of the stone inside the stalk.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks soon, and flies out with the urine, then the patient is healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that hinders it, then tie a thread below the stone and another above it, then cut the stalk at the stone between the two threads, then pull it out with forceps, untie the thread, and clean the blood clot from the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	"from the stone of women"
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It happens rarely that a stone enters the bladder of women; and if it does happen sometimes, its treatment is difficult and forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a well-known woman who reveals herself to physicians, especially if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third manner is that perhaps one cannot find a skilled woman in this art of midwery;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth manner is that the stones of the woman are more hidden than those of a man, for which one must make a deeper cut, causing great fear. And if you need to show them, then you must take a skilled midwife, and they are scarcely found, and if you do not find any, seek out a very learned and subtle female physician;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and the present one brings a very wise old woman knowledgeable in women's affairs or a woman who knows some part of this art, and commands her to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and observe carefully whether the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	Then he must place his thumb on the foundation and search for the stone.
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And if he finds it, let him press down on it with his thumb, and tell the patient to place their hand over the bladder, and then grasp and press strongly with their left hand.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she must move it little by little from the entrance of the bladder until it reaches the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then strike the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the anus where it has moved, and feel for the stone in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	And do not move your thumb above or below the stone, but make the first cut small.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then insert the knife into the cut. If you feel the stone, widen the wound until the stone can exit. Know that there are many types of stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	That is to say, some are small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and some have tails.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	and know the similitudes to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if your blood weakens, then place powdered vitriol in its place, holding it for an hour until the blood is stanched.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work until the stone is removed, having instruments that I told you about for extracting stones in men to help you with your task;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if blood weakens you, and this is from a cut artery, then place the powder on the spot and hold it with bandages and strips, do not resume cutting, leave the stone and do not extract it at all, for fear that the patient might die;
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	"And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the wound is healed, then return to your task until the stone is out."
de hernie carnouse	Hernia carnosum
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Rainwater is nothing other than a collection of moisture or clear urine, which is below the heart of hens and contains eggs;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called "syfac," but sometimes it is pure in the fabric of the egg itself, so one might think it was another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and this is the skin of the pig between the white sinew which we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And if it's not hot, then no.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	"And the generation of this hernia is from weakness that comes to the intestines, and this matter is spread out."
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	Sometimes it comes from a blow to the joints, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	Or it is colored declining towards yellow, or it is without redness, or black, or aqueous white, and there are more.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this gathering: if it is white like the sinew we have mentioned, then the abscess is solid and long like the shape of an egg, and it does not open the joints because it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in its own skin, then the abscess is solid with a part of the egg white, and because of this people think it's another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	If the moisture is between the skin of the joints and the white sinew, then one feels it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, try all four corners of the surrounding area where the form is shown beforehand.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	"So according to what comes after the probe, judge what is inside."
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cauterize it with iron, it is necessary for the patient to be as healthy as possible and his body well-fed.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	Then lay him on his back on something slightly raised, and place many cloths underneath him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on the left side of the patient, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right side, and extend the staff to one of the two ribs on the right side of the chest.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the scalpel and cut through the skin of the chest along the line from the nipple to near the armpit, making a straight incision that divides the skin down to the white fat, scraping it off carefully according to your ability;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the fat with water using a large needle, extract all the water, and then place your bandages, stretching the skin upwards;
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	And do not touch the heart of the chest, but only the skin.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cut through all or in pieces the costal cartilage from below carefully, so that if you do not cut it sharply enough, water will flow back.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg jumps out of your way, replace it in its place once you have completed the task.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then join the two books of the heart of the lungs with stitches, then heal it like other wounds until it is sound.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then tie up the vessels that are suspended, preventing the flow of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the lung with all its suspension and remove the egg, and heal it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if water is gathered into two parts together, know that these are two branches.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	So cut the other part equally as you did the first, then suck out the blood, and put linen moistened in rose oil on the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And put another linen moistened in wine and oil on top, place it over both lungs, cover with doubled cloths, and tie it all together according to this pattern:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two strips of cloth, and stuff them with wool bandages in this manner, and they should be sewn together at the waistband of the breeches, and one end should be taken up from the fundament to the back, and the other at the wrist.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and tie both ends together over the two angles, so that the bandage is fully assembled in the loop of the breeches;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this bandage is used as a cautery in place of iron tongs; you should take one small scalpel cautery and scrape the skin around the boil, and heat it up as we have said, so that the white fat which contains water is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	then take this cautery in this manner and pierce that fat at its base with it, and scrape off the boil with this hot scalpel cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And scrape it all away in every way you can, until everything is scraped clean.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	And make sure that the fire does not touch the eye
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	And know that this work is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and avoid blood loss during the operation; make sure the cutting process is done carefully;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if anything goes against you, such as a wound becoming inflamed or excessive bleeding or other issues, then treat what is going against you according to what is said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its frightening nature, then perform a perforation, as I tell you; for when you are certain by the signs that we have mentioned that the kidney stone is there, then make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then cut open the abscess on the part below to the whole spinal region widely, and insert the perforation deep into the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And make the opening wide enough so that all the water flows out freely;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton on the wound and tie it, and leave it to allow the remaining water to flow out, then treat it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow water to exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the tool used for drawing out water in hydropics, as shown above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And widen the mouth of the wound, and know that water returns, and after six months or more it reassembles, and when it reassembles as before, then the patient will pass their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the boil on the buttocks
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the cutting of this branch there is fear and many dangers, therefore it seems better to leave it alone;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	I will tell you about the treatment and the like of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say therefore that many abscesses come to be in the body, especially in the joints;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this happens often.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is known that this is due to an excess of acid and water spread throughout the joints, or from injury;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	And does not find any pain, but an abscess severe.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And sometimes there is a pale and bloody abscess, yellowish in color, often caused by an artery's wound or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from an artery wound, it is known by the hot arrangement of the abscess when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And do not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which is caused by vein swelling is known by its expression when touched with the fingers, and can be well incised in this manner and others.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And cut the skin of the shin bones, then stretch them out, and the egg-shaped swelling will appear white on its surface, and remove the suspending membrane from all around the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hard with these new growths, then you must extract the egg and cut it;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is air-filled on its surface or inside the vessels, then you must remove all that membrane and cut it cleanly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the origin of the flesh is at the back, you must cut it all away, and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your operations are complete, apply linen soaked in rose oil and wine to the wound, then dress it with other dressings until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the boil on the buttocks
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapping resembling a boil, with softening of the kidneys, and if the patient moves they cry out.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment of this disease is equally frightening as the one mentioned earlier; nonetheless, we will tell you about it according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You should have the patient sit on an elevated seat, then place the suspension of the kidneys below their testicles, close to the penis and scrotum, and the master should hold them tautly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut with a sharp, wide-bladed scalpel across the vessels until they are exposed and then scrape each side as we have described in the extraction of arteries from the temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then insert a needle with a doubled thread and tie it at the first spot where the vessel appeared, then tie it again at the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut straight through the middle, according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound like others where an arrow is struck, so that none of the vessels fall out from either side.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For otherwise no harm comes of it, and if all the vessels are visible, then you must pull on both sides of the wound for all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the bone does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot heal.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the nose
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The outcome of this operation is that it results in the sectioning that comes from below, or the extension upwards on the abdomen in the region of the groin, causing the intestines to descend through that opening on one side
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this opening is either below the scrotum or from its extension, and both these methods are caused by many things
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from blows, falls, jumps, carrying heavy loads, and similar causes
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the sign when it is due to the extension of the scrotum is that it happens gradually over a long period of time, and does not come suddenly
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscess is even to its depth because the surgeon presses the intestine
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign when it is a cut in the thigh is that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are various visible swellings under the skin, which is due to the leakage of intestines and blood from the wound in the thigh
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	Sometimes the rings are torn along with the intestines, which are retained inside and cause great suffering for the sick person, especially when they are pressed upon
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cases of iron wounds, it is necessary to avoid them
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	The manner of this procedure is that you should instruct the patient to replace the intestine with their hand inside the wound, if it can be reached.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then gently press on its colon between your hands and raise the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then stretch out the heart upwards and cut all the skin from the length of the thighs
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then insert forceps into the hips on each side according to your need to open the wound, so that the bone can come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then skin the surgeon so that it is under the skin of the thighs until the white muscle is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your index fingers into that which supports the thigh, between the white muscle that is beneath the skin of the egg (scrotum), and the second muscle, and separate what lies behind the egg, and between the second muscle
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then move your right hand into the heart of the kidneys, and stretch your left hand upwards to touch the spleen, and lift the eye towards the waist.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	And instruct the assistant to raise the eye upwards, and untie that which is behind the lien.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And search with your two hands if there is any intestine wrapped around or hard spleen, and if you find anything, push it into the abdomen below.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a thick thread made of silk threads and insert it into the rear part of the spleen, which is after the kidney's skin.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	Afterwards, cut the heads that appear from the threads, until there are four threads remaining;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then tie them together in the form of a cross and tie the spleen, which we have said is below the kidney's skin, with a strong thread in two parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the heads of the threads and tie them firmly in two parts so that no vessels that nourish it can enter inside, so that an abscess may not come.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And then place the bandage according to the first bandage's length of two fingers from that one, and after these two bandages leave the sinew that is under the heart of the lungs on the right side.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	And then the rest according to the roundness that the arm carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	Then cut into the part that is under the skin of the lungs until blood flows and the bowels, as we have said before;
