puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then bring wool moistened in oil and place it on the wounds, and then bring the bandage that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes cauterize the white flesh that we have mentioned after the incision, for fear of bleeding
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	But this happened many times, so leave the bandage until it sticks by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	And if it is slow to stick, then be risen with warm water and place on what we have said until it sticks;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then treat the wound with another cure until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	Hernia carnosum
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I never saw anyone daring to perform the cure by iron
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it should be done like the branch that grows with the vine, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting slightly above lightly below;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut in mid-air, and treat the boil of he who operates, until the vessels bleed.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it as we have said, until it is healthy.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a rupture occurs in angles, as we have said, and the place opens up;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	And none of the intestines descend to the joints, and if any do, it is little, and repair them at all times.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	But if it remains too long in this state, the wound becomes inflamed or gangrenous, so that the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens due to the extension of the gangrene which is at the angles, as we have said, for it extends, then the place becomes softened and swollen and opens up.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And its treatment is by cautery, as we have previously said.
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And sometimes it is cured by iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And the patient should lie on their back between your hands, then cut the place of the rupture open with a wide incision according to the size of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	And then remove the sinew that is under the skin which you follow, then take the thread and place it on the visible surface of the sinew.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press deeply into the abdomen, then sew the two visible surfaces of the sinew onto the top of the thread, sewing one and the other.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then remove the top of the thread, and do not cover any part of the sinew or extend the wound or anything else, as I have shown you in the treatment of intestinal rupture.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat it with the cure for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, cleanse and dress the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The sinew is contracted and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cautery is more effective at this point and closer to safety.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	Regarding the softening of the skin around the anus
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often in some men the skin of the scrotum becomes softened because the contents inside are softened to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one wants to treat it, for the patient to lie on his back, and cut away the softened skin from the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then bring together both lips with one stitch, and if you wish, sew up the excess softened skin with three or four firm stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the ribs, and heal it like other wounds until it is healed, and then stitch it up.
dou chastrement	Regarding castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that astrologers are condemned in our law, therefore I would like to not speak about them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	And it is necessary to mention for only two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	One of which is so that the physician may know how to answer when asked and how to treat;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	And the other is because we often have need of castration for certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	Either by traction or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the first way, which we do by traction, make the animal sit in warm water until its testicles are softened and hanging down;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then grasp them with your hand so that they remain in place and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the cautery of burns:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	You must shear the animal, and press its skin with your left hand, then tie the suspender, and cut each boil once when you have well cleaned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave any boil that is deep and hidden beneath the vessels.
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this method of cauterization is better than that done by suction because some substances from the boils may remain through suction, which causes the animal to crave lustfulness.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Regarding hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism exists in two ways among men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One way is that between the two testicles appears also the form of a woman's genitals, with hair and sometimes urine comes out through the foreskin.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way is in women, who have on their pubic region both a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for both men and women is that you cut away all the excess skin, and heal it like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second way, there are men whose urine flows through the foreskin's skin, for whom there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	Regarding hemorrhoids：
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tartaric acid is a substance applied to the natural part, so it looks too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary for you to cut off the excess skin of the tenting with scissors, then trim it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then apply the treatment until it is healthy again.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And there is another substance that arises from the mouth of the uterus, and the womb, and sometimes jumps out, and resembles a cow's udder, and for this reason the ancients called it 'cow-like disease'.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must cut it, as we have said regarding the tenting procedure, and care for it until it is healthy.
de erratique	Of the erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic is when a woman's nature is not pierced, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural at birth, or accidental due to illness that comes upon it.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is caused by applied flesh, or a thick or thin membrane, and it is formed deeply in the uterus, on the sides, below, or wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	And forbids conception, childbirth, and sometimes flowers from being had.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	And the recognition of these is by the gaze of the woman.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swelling is near the surface, then search with your fingers or a probe.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is close and subtle, and near the two books, then be quick, they are together like this:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Bring your two index fingers together, and let the woman be on her back with her legs spread.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then open the two books together until the subtle vulva is revealed, and cover the openings.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, soak it in oil, place it on the location, and let the woman lie on her stomach each day so that it does not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the shoulder blade is hard and thick, you must shave it like a laurel leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the opening is born from flesh, then stretch it with the horn and cut it open;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have the blood-stopping medicines ready, such as achic, dragon's blood, incense, mixed with an egg.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then prepare a wide leaden funnel so that the wound cannot heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And thus let it be lengthened, and provide him with a linen tent.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then other treatments should be applied until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when flesh comes out in the wound, it must be shaved in this manner, unless it's an inflamed abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For the inflamed abscess that is in the wound, one should not apply fire.
des emorroides	**Hemorrhoids:** Hemorrhoids are varicose veins inside or outside the anus; they appear as small lumps like bunches of grapes; some are internal and invisible from without, while others are external; they cause pain when defecating or sitting down; they can cause blood to flow freely during defecation or after, or only stain the toilet paper; sometimes they prolapse and come out at defecation; they are caused by constipation due to a bad diet, heavy lifting, or frequent diarrhea. The cure for them is to avoid their causes: eat healthy food that does not cause constipation, drink plenty of water, exercise regularly, do not lift heavy objects unnecessarily, and use ointments to relieve pain and inflammation. For internal hemorrhoids, surgery may be necessary if they are large or causing significant symptoms. Otherwise, rubber band ligation, sclerotherapy, or infrared coagulation can be used to treat them. For external hemorrhoids, warm sitz baths, witch hazel pads, and over-the-counter creams can provide relief. In severe cases, surgery may be necessary.
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that do not normally occur in this way; and when hemorrhoids become old they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	As we have already said in the division of them, their similitudes and signs; now I will say those that require treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and piles, when they are deeply embedded in the flesh, and are not visible to the touch, then iron treatment is not applicable.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the anus, which one can feel, those are the ones that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore you should put the woman in a cold house, then grasp the hemorrhoids with forceps, cut them at their root, and sprinkle powders containing sanguinary-restraining medicines on it, such as achiote and dragon's blood, incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then place her feet in cold water for an hour, then put her in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if there is bleeding, then make her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, and similar things; then take barley flour, mix it with honey and oil, and apply this poultice on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if she stops bleeding, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not this, then apply cupping glasses to the back and breasts without piercing.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take linen, dampen it in burdock juice or celandine juice with old wine, and apply to the location.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has softened, then treat the area with ointment until it is clean;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles a sharp-pointed head, so it must be covered as I said earlier;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	**Abscesses of the Rectum:** Abscesses of the rectum are localized collections of pus that can develop due to infection or injury to the tissues of the anorectal area. Symptoms may include pain, swelling, redness, warmth, and fever. Treatment typically involves incision and drainage of the abscess under local anesthesia to relieve pressure and allow the pus to drain out. This procedure is usually performed by a surgeon or colorectal specialist. If the abscess is deep-seated or associated with significant inflammation, the patient may require intravenous antibiotics to fight infection and prevent it from spreading. In some cases, a seton (a loop of suture material) may be placed into the abscess cavity to allow for ongoing drainage over time. It's important to note that untreated abscesses can rupture spontaneously, causing severe pain and potentially leading to serious complications such as sepsis or fistula formation. Therefore, prompt medical attention is crucial for proper diagnosis and treatment.
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of boils come in the flesh, such as cancer and stone boil, herpes and erysipelas and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot boil, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I must speak of the hot abscess that comes in the marrow, which is not one of those that swell;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron, look whether the abscess is hot at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore, do not rush to pierce it, but let it ripen until the pain is alleviated;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then make the patient sit on the seat, and have two small seats where they can recline, and lean them against their back and bring their feet together near the knee.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let their thighs be spread out, and place their arms beneath their knees, and tie them securely with a good binding;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then have the helper approach from the right side and bring forth the instrument with which one opens the mouth of the mare, the form of which shall follow.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you bring forth this instrument, you first insert the rod to know the depth of the mare's throat, so that what enters thereafter does not go deeper than it should and injure the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	And if the instrument is too large, then cover the depth of the mare's throat with cloths so that the instrument does not cause injury.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	And it is necessary for him to put the funnel of the instrument on top and moisten the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when an abscess opens, and you cut it gently by hand, then it is necessary to cover its head with spathumile lotion.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	And when the bowels are emptied, then you should put into the wound moistened tents in rose oil or green oil set.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	And place the tent far from the wound at the bottom of the marrow, and put behind it on the marrow and on the linen cloth moistened with hot water or malted water.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it afterwards for 2 days with appropriate ointment until it is sound.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	And sometimes lift up the marrow and wound by enema of water and honey, then with water in which lily roots and long aristolochia are cooked.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	Then reapply the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is located in the marrow, then you must refrain from cauterizing with fire, but treat it as we have said in the section on dislocations.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	The task of the midwife is first to know the form of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman pressing downwards, and she desires to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	Then the child eagerly desires to come out (into the world).
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	Then know that this birth is according to Nature's form; the head comes out first, followed by the child.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, gently press his belly so that the child may come out quickly
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	For when it settles upon its head, then comes forth the afterbirth with it; and the mother is cleansed of her excesses through proper cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	And any child that comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes out on its feet, with the body or head first, or the hands; or it may come out on its belly, and sometimes it is turned around by chance on its neck or in other harmful positions
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	Therefore, it is necessary that the midwife be wise and skillful in these matters, careful to avoid error or deception; and I shall show you all the positions and how one should assist her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out naturally headfirst and the woman is crying out in pain, but her contractions are weak, then have her sit on a stool or have women hold her up
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	And if the nature of oil or fenugreek has been cooked, then place the small spatula between its teeth, of which here is the form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	And cut the foreskin, and scrape with its nail until the moisture within flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And take the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then the woman must be given a suppository of ground fenugreek with sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her inhale the powder and sneeze, holding her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	The child will now be born.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out first, then you must gently push them back in bit by bit;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot be pushed back in, then put the woman on a seat and raise her feet high.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then lower the seat to the ground, taking care that the woman does not fall during this process;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if the hands cannot be pushed in and the child is dead, then cut the hands at the joint shown here and extract the child, resetting it correctly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	Of the delivery of a child onto its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes onto his feet, then you must strike upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it gently, gently, until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take one of the feet and extend it gently, gently.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When he jumps up to his knees, then command him to grasp it, and make him sneeze with rue;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If God wills, let him jump forth.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if there is no cautery as we have said, then it should be turned little by little until it matches its natural shape
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Then it becomes easy
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if he does not come out as we have said, then take musk mallow from the mountain, and oil of sesame, and melted gum, and grind everything together in one mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	And apply this ointment to the nature of the woman, then have her sit in hot water up to below her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	And when she is softened below, put on the woman a girdle of myrrh and place it under her, leaving it for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	Then have her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose closed, and lightly press her belly, for the child will now come out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	"of the child's exit onto its knees"
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When a child comes in this form, then the bailiff puts his hands gently.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	and is hung by the neck, with legs hanging down, lying on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and folds his hands gently, then he takes the hands onto the stomach, and removes the cushions underneath so that it hangs down properly;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, he takes its feet and shakes them violently, then moves his stomach up, then places his hands there;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and takes the child gently;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and tells the woman to hold on until the child is born.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	"One hand comes out during the birth of the child"
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to devise how to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If it cannot be brought back, then make the woman get up and go;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot go, then make her lie on the bed, and forcefully lift her legs;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the muscle relaxant that I have mentioned.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, make her sit on the chair, then study how to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	And swaddle the child according to its natural shape, then make it sneeze, and instruct her to lie on her back until the child is freed.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	"At the moment of birth, with its hands spread wide, facing its mother's back."
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the servant take his hand, then slowly turn it little by little, and swaddle it lightly;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is aligned, then place the natural balsamic mixture of mastic and oil on it, as we have said, then instruct her to move it slowly;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on the seat, and instruct her to lie down;
et la fai esternuer.	And make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	"This same manner is used for the afterbirth."
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes free in this manner from the entire afterbirth, then cut the afterbirth with your fingernail until all moisture is drained;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child's face and neck are covered in blood, then cut it at the cheek, so that it is not retained, otherwise the child will die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then place the child inside until you have positioned it correctly, and instruct the woman to lie on her back several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	Then it can be eased gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	"Regarding the birth of twins:"
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are often born, sometimes three or four at a time;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it happens occasionally.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are rare, and do not live long, if they have names;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know those that are multiplied, and they are despised by the devil who divides them, which is tied to hunger.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out naturally like one whole, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are born crying, the treatment is as we have said, and the midwife should be skilled, and do what she does quickly and easily;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do it in such a way that it leads to health.
de plusors enfans	"Regarding multiple births:"
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb two or three or four or five or six or seven, or many up to fifteen, and all of them are perfectly shaped like children according to the measure of God's glory, and it is necessary that the midwife knows all these things, for such things can happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	If one does according to what is necessary
de l’enfant mort	Regarding a stillborn child:
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman for a dead child or miscarriage, as I have described in the section on this topic, and it does not expel the fetus, you are constrained to intervene manually
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	Then you must know whether the woman is of sound virtue, and has no illness or fears death
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	Then the woman should be positioned on her back with her head lowered and her legs raised
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the assistant should grasp her thighs, or she should be tied to the bed so that she cannot push during childbirth
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the womb with moist oils made from althea and fenugreek and linseed, then anoint your hands with these oils and mucilages
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then gently insert your hands into the womb, then find the place where you can grasp the handles that are suitable for this purpose, and be careful that if the child is in the breech position it does not slip out headfirst
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If he sticks the arrows in his eyes or in his neck or in his mouth or on his palate or under the beard or in the belly or near the ribs, and if the descent is below feet, stick them or prick them at the middle ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And he must draw the arrow with his right hand, place the curve between the fingers of his left hand, and gently push it with all his strength, sticking the arrow into any of these places that we have mentioned, until the object is emptied.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the arrow:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then stick against the other arrow, or the third if you need it, so that the extractions are even.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then stretch them evenly by moving from one side to the other, so that they can come out easily, and let the arrows be toothed for better grip, as shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if there remains a part of it, then oil some of his fingers with oil and press them on that part, and pull the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	If none remains there, then place this poultice higher up, and do so until it completely emits fire.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other and cannot return due to constraint, you must wrap it with cloth until it relaxes completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then strike the joint of the sole or the instep, and do likewise for the other foot.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and its passage narrow, or has a sharp-pointed bone assembled at its forehead, you must place the spatha spine between your two index fingers and cut open the forehead and extract the bone.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you could round it using the instrument called "almidach", for which the form comes with the instruments in the chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do likewise if the child has naturally a large head;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	Then draw out the bones with forceps, and if the head still resists and is constrained by the forceps, cut it until the moisture in the pectoral opening escapes.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot come out, cut it into pieces with a knife where you can reach.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	If it is swollen in the belly or beneath the ribs, then you must pierce it until the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	"And if the child is on its feet, traction will be light, and the alignment of the mouth of the marrow will be easy."
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is stuck in the belly or the breast, then you must pull it out using a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut into the belly or the breast until the moisture that is inside runs out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if other bones are broken but the head remains in place, then put your hand deep into the marrow and draw it out until you reach the mouth of the marrow.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then put in a hot poultice or two, and burn it with fire.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the mouth of the marrow is narrowed due to an inflamed ulcer that has come there, then you should not work it open, but rather bring moist and fatty substances
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and use plasters, and make poultices from softening and moistening herbs.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can set it right, then arrange as we have said in the living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	If one has no power, then let it flee by pieces; leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if arrangements should come to abscesses that arise in the flesh.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	If blood flows, let it be put into restricted water, and arrange other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	"I saw a woman whose child had been bitten in the abdomen by one mouse, then another mouse came and bit the other."
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	"After many days, an abscess formed on her cheekbone and swelled so much that it opened up, causing great pain."
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	"I was called to treat her, but after thinking about it for some time, I could not heal the wound."
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	"I applied a poultice with strong drawing power and out came one bone, then after a few days another."
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	"I was greatly amazed at this because the abdomen has no bones."
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	"So I thought it must be the bones of a dead fetus."
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I wished the wound to be wide, and pulled out many bones until the woman was much improved;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And the woman lived for a long time like this, and sometimes a little bone would come out.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	I recorded this chapter so that when the master finds something unusual, he may know how to help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	"on bringing the hip joint back into place"
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Hereafter comes the form of the compresses, according to which the books are opened;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And at two turns for each head of the kidneys.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, let the wedge be more subtle than the restrictor, and made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And let the mouth of the wood be two fingers wide, and the margin of the trees one and a half palms long.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And in the middle let there be two joints of this same wood, which are closed on one and open on the other, half a palm long or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two joints are placed in the mouth of the mallet to open it when one turns the two wedges.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood wood, according to the shape of the tweezers.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	And it has at each end two joints, as you see, one palm long and two fingers wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	And when you wish to open the mallet with all the equipment, make the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging down and her legs spread wide apart, then insert the two joints joined together into the mallet, and hold the head of the equipment under her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then open your hand to the instrument, just as you did with the pliers evenly, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the mortar, until the pestle does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This tool is all equal, and their appearances are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the master has prepared them, the quicker the work is done, and the higher it rises among people for its quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	"Therefore do not disregard the instrument until you have prepared it, for its usefulness is not negligible."
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second twin is retained during childbirth, you must command the woman to retain her breath, and then make her sneeze with condition, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she sneezes because of it, all is well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take the pot, and make a hole in the lid, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the mortar, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cumin, and centory;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in water over fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a tube through the hole of the pot, with the other end in the mouth of the person sick, and hold it thus until the vapors enter the person;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then cause them to sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	"If the midwife acts quickly,"
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and is not extinguished, command the maiden to moisten her left hand in oil of sesame or in gum arabic, then place it on the navel and rub the second bellybutton.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, grasp it and stretch it little by little straight out, so that the person does not fall during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But one must move it gently to the right and left, then pull it out.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes out and becomes disconnected.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the person's mouth is narrow, we have given the treatment of sneezing and herb fumigation;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it is not as we have said, then guard that you do not err in bleeding.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the uterus, you tie it to the thigh of the woman, then perform a vaginal irrigation with a tetrafarmacon ointment.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	Then she will swell and revert, and come back stronger.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But nonetheless, when it swells and there comes a bad smell to the stomach and head, then it wounds the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, fume incense suitable for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	A number of the ancients have tested fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	"The shape of the instrument used for fumigation of the woman during childbirth and delivery is as follows:"
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is similar in appearance to a dog's tail, and one places the fine point on the nature, and the wide heads over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigation be over the charcoal embers until it is exhausted, then begin another.
de percier lou fondement	"to pierce the anus"
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born whose anus is not pierced but obstructed by some small membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If it must then be, that the maid shall prick him with a needle at his hand, and not with a sharp point, she should clean the thread first so as not to touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place damp linen soaked in wine and oil on it, then apply the salve until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	"And if you suspect that it has not healed, insert a silver tube into the hole and leave it there for several days. It should be removed when the child is ready to go to its room."
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this swelling arises suddenly from a wound or abscess.
si covient coper celui soudement:	If that suddenness must be covered:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	As we have said about the burn of boiling water.
de la fistule dou fondement	"of a fistula of the anus"
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that arise beneath the fundament are nodular, and growths that arise near the fundament or in the space between the two buttocks indicate the presence of one fistula or more.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when this nodulation is ancient and opens up, it oozes moist white pus or subtle bowels, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are recognized by the fact that fluid or wind comes out during evacuation when the patient defecates, and sometimes a worm jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that pierce up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they reach as far as the hip joint, and as high as the nape of the neck.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a fistula piercing into the fundament, but not piercing:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you place your two index fingers on the fundament, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twists, then insert a thin reed or horsehair into the fistula until you feel the reed or hair with your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and nothing comes out of the hole except wind or vapor, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not pierce.
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to cure [it].
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	"And when a fistula extends all the way to the bladder or the urethra, urine flows out of it and cannot be stopped with medications."
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced as far as the hip joint, then the reed coming from there reaches the place:
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twisting and the pain does not spread around, then it has left suddenly, and medication or salves are of no avail.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	In these Persian fistulas there is no other cure but labor, and foolishness of those physicians who meddle with them in vain.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	For that which is not Persian and not ancient, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have proven, and it is necessary for the patient to lie on their back between your hands.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And lift up his legs until his thighs are level with his belly
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then place an iron tent on it, or lead if there is twisting, until you know where the tent enters.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must insert your two index fingers there, until you sense that the tent has pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And when you feel between your fingers the sinew or flesh, know then that it is Persian.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If one does not work at it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said everywhere that some can indeed be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that one does there, it is to heat the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as it was said earlier;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and insert it hot into the fistula until it reaches the base;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times until you know that these broken parts have been burnt off, which resemble the feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then rinse with damp cloths until that charred part comes off, and then apply an ointment between the skin and the wound to heal it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is healed thus, all the better.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters but does not pierce all the way to the bone that is at the base, and between your two fingers and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or fat, and you see the fistula through the covering on the heart side;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If at the start of the fistula, you grab and pull forward the skin, then apply the cautery afterwards until it reaches the tip of the skin.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the skin will be relieved, and it will fall off;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then scrape away those faulty parts that resemble a bird's feather, leaving none behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	"If the skin becomes inflamed, and cracks between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or strong medicine."
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery accomplishes two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of those attached parts, and the staunching of blood and the drying out of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment for moist skin sores with hot ashes or crushed substances until the wound gapes wide open, and the burned skin can be pulled out from the wound;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with solid oils that penetrate deep into the flesh, and these are dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	"For when it is thus restored, it will be healed and not return again."
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	"And if the fistula comes right up from the fundament but is distant from the body, push your thumb into the fundament and feel with it."
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel that the skin is about to burst between two stitches or sutures or flesh, where there is great danger and hope, then administer one of three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	When you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it down to the bottom, if you can then apply dressings and heal it as first.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too deep that you cut the tissue holding the fundament, and cause unwanted discharge.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then heal it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	Perhaps then it will be healed, or you remove that covering and cleanse it after it has been cut near the fundament, either with a dressing or with some other pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse the faulty flesh in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then strive to restore the wound and ensure the fistula remains towards the front of the fundament
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	so that it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are formed in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and when you insert the dressing into the fistula and it is on the side of the fundament near the skin above, then take a pointed dressing shaped like this:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	"And thread two turns of thread onto it, then insert the tent all the way down to its tip into the fistula."
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces through to the margin of the foundation within, then extract the thread from that hole, in such a way as you would push your finger into the foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And pull out the head of the thread, and bring together the two heads, and tie one to the other, leaving it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And bind it several times until the threads break those excesses that are between them.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then dress the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	"If the fistula does not open on its own, then make an incision in any way that you can, if it is not too deep."
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"For one should not cut too deeply for the sake of making a hole and then dress it as we have described until it is healed."
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spatula used for opening a fistula should be narrow, pointed, and cutting-edge;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other side not so, because one should not break what one should not break, as you see here:
des emorroydes	"hemorrhoids"
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Haemorrhoids are of two kinds
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Either they are inside the fundament like grains of resin and are small or large in size; there is blood present on their surface at all times, and there may be one or several, they deform the fundament and its head
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those which are displaced have little moisture, often containing a bit of yellow citrine or a bit of blood, and they have the color of flesh.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those which are in the fundament, so it is that you command the patient to strain while walking around rooms, until the fundament is released, and they become visible.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	So hurry, and take it with tongs or hold it with your fingernail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the tweezers cannot hold them due to their moisture, then take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	Then pull them out with your thumbs, then cut them off, and sprinkle warm powders on them in place of cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the fundament cannot be released, then administer a bitter and sharp enema to wash out whatever is in the fundament so that it can be released openly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient grabs [it], and if the hairs are burned at their base, then the treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should grasp them with your nail or with forceps, cut them off, then cauterize them as we have said, until they are clean and the patient fears cutting by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	If you must arrange stitching in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread, insert it into a needle, then draw the thread up and pierce the needle from the other side, turn both ends of the thread under the needle, and thus make it wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And draw the thread tautly, then tie the knot, remove the needle, and do so for all others, leaving one for checking excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the wound a moist cloth soaked in rose oil or wax, and cover it, instructing the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And leave it thus until they fall off, and when they have fallen off, treat them with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	"on the drying of fistulas in the fundament"
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	"Sometimes there is a drying up of fistulas in the intestines due to constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine no longer helps;"
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If you must scrape off with a scalpel's tip or your nail the scab above it that moisture does not remain.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then dress it until it becomes firm as is fitting;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot become firm, then resume scraping more forcefully than before, until much blood flows and the flesh is scraped raw.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then dress it until it becomes clean.
dou fremit	fever
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Formice (formication) is a small apparition that occurs before the body and goes very deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it finds the limbs cold, with a sensation like deathly trembling, spreading throughout the whole body, especially in the hands more than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from an eagle's wing or a strong owl's feather, and place this feather on the trembling spot until the circle formed around it becomes red.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then twist your hand around the entire feather until you encompass the trembling spot completely and drive it deep within, crushing its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	"And if you see this, do so with a cane of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be thin underneath and pointed above:"
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Does not pierce, to keep movement steady, and presses on the two sides.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, cauterize around the trembling, as it is written in the chapter of cauteries
de la forme dou clistere	"of the form of the enema"
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes, one performs an enema with silver or lead, or molten brass or copper;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these instruments are made small and large according to those for whom they are intended.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	"Therefore, those that should be used in the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful are small."
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	"The form of the small and large enema is as follows, where the belly is tied according to this manner:"
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is a constriction or the belly is bound up, as you see, and the bowels are pierced within;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and on one side there are two holes, and on the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And the belly should be filled with medicines in a beast's bladder or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes, and between each hole there should be one finger's width of space, then insert strong threads of coarse yarn twisted in an X shape or wound around, and gather up the belly like a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument beforehand with a strong thread, then cauterize.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and grease the end of the cautery with oil or egg yolk, or something similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister presses with both hands together until it is all flat, then extracts the cautery, and the patient raises their legs to the side, and if the medicine wants to come out, let it come as much as it can;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he spends a night entirely undisturbed, it is greater aid.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if you perform an enema on someone with diarrhea and the medication comes out quickly, then start it again until it is finished."
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament or in an abscess, let the cautery be as fine as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the shape of the fine cautery on which the skin should be stretched:
des plaies	"wounds."
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already spoken in the division about the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	I shall tell you the treatments for hands and medicines according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	"I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to where the wounds are made, and what they are made from."
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by striking with stone, cutting with sword and knife or lance, club or arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or wounds made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, head, thigh, belly, liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, starting with simple head wounds, as memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, take care if it was caused by striking with stone or similar things, and if the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, then you greatly doubt the formation of a hot abscess
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	then quickly wash it with cold water from the head itself if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the washing be contrary to the direction of the wound;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And when the patient has emptied themselves of wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to fast, then let his food be made smaller, and let him drink no wine nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place upon the wound, if an abscess forms, cotton moistened in rose oil alone, or in astringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no hot abscess, then place over the wound, if it is fresh and full of blood and not moved by air, powder which I will describe later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the air has moved it, then place on it some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	"And if the wound is large, like a cut from a sword or similar objects, and the lips cannot be brought together by force, then bring them together by stitching, as I will tell you about in the treatment of abdominal wounds."
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to the bone and gaping, and hangs only by a little, cut it off;
