puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	Then examine each joint on the third day after bandaging to ensure that no itching or inflammation occurs there, so that the healing cannot come to the limb because it is too tight.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	If the hip joint, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if no such accidents occur, then do not untie the bandage until after three days or more, and let the patient sleep on their back with their hands on their stomach.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	and place underneath the shoulder-blade one cushion filled with even wool, and watch every hour of the day or night that the shape of the broken limb does not move or the bandages become softened.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	If by the power of medicine the patient recovers, and receives the food that we have mentioned earlier, let it be administered in such a way that the food is first softened.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	And when it begins to heal, let it be thick.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	It is customary that the arm and leg should be reset after forty days in total;
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	Then, one should untie it and apply baths and ointment medicines to direct it to its proper place.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the dislocation is severe and stuck, let it remain dislocated for forty days or two months.
de la brisure du bras	Here is an English translation of the French text about the treatment of a broken arm:
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is composed of two bones called the 'fossae', one of which is small and supports the elbow;
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	and the other is large and lies beneath towards the little finger;
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	Sometimes only the large 'fossa' breaks, or sometimes only the small one, and sometimes both together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	If the small 'fossa' is broken, the restoration will be easy, and healing will occur;
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	But if the large one is broken, then healing will be poor, and more grievous than when they are both broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If only the small bone is broken, it should be gently straightened and aligned.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it's the large 'fossa', it must be pulled harder;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	And extend [it] upon the cushion; draw back the pouch of the hand higher than the others, and let the little finger be lower than the other fingers, and let the patient be crossed over themselves, and the cushion should be in front of them so that the patient feels no discomfort.
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	Then extend the minister's strong arm to the part below his hand or elbow; another minister should be placed above it.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	And then the doctor should set it straight according to its natural shape.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if in the fracture there are pieces, place each one in its proper place; and if there is any misplaced piece that touches the heart, and you cannot restore it to its place, then cut it off and remove the bone, as we have said before.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with breaking open a wound, I have spoken about that in the specific chapter
si pren la cure.	then take care
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if at the beginning of recovery boils appear, then apply a cloth of cerote made from rose oil and white wax, so that it is not too hard nor too soft;
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and bind the cloth gently until the boil is relieved.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	And then remove the cerote, and place the plaster of the powder of millet with abundance of egg yolk; then apply the bandages, and let the bandage of the wound be always stronger and a little wider than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	And you shall know that he ought to have six braces on his arm in various positions:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	Whether the break is in one bone or two;
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	And bound more tightly above the fracture than elsewhere, and less so when aligning it, as I said at the beginning of this chapter;
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	And let the bandages that are on the fracture be soft and moist, not hard or harsh;
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	Let the thread used for binding be of linen, neither too thick nor too thin, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And reward the limb and the bandage after a few days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if any bad accident comes to the limb, such as itching that comes to the limb, then you should bathe the limb with hot water until that itching is soothed;
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the limb rest not too tightly.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	And then recommences the stretching, and if the ligaments are softened and the bones dislocated, and similar things, adjust it.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses .i. poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if care is taken that the healing cannot come to the limb because it is too tight, then you should loosen it a little and leave it like that for some days until the healing reaches it, and then bind it again.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things that we have said come to the patient, then do not untie him for up to 20 days.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	And whoever is around should then wrap his hands around his neck, and keep them even; he should guard against movement and trembling, and sleep on his back;
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	And know that this dislocation is healed in thirty days or thirty-five, and perhaps in twenty days, according to the compositions and complexions of the virtues.
de la brisure de la main	Chapter 18: On the Fracture of the Hand
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Know that on the back of the hand and on our elbows there are few fractures, and only then do they occur frequently.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the palm of the hand is dislocated or folded, it is necessary for the patient to sit cross-legged and sit upright directly before him evenly.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	Then he places his hand on the extended towel, and the ministers extend the broken bones, and the physician joins them evenly, so they are properly aligned.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	And he applies the emplaster and bandages, if an abscess does not form, then he places a splint according to the quantity of the location.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	and it should be wrapped in one linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the dislocation is around the wrist on the palm side, then make a splint of cloth and instruct the patient to bind it tightly to their injured palm.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	And then he binds it with a long cloth strip, and the splint should be of soft wood as large as the palm of the hand, binding it as necessary.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is on the outside, then a roller should be placed on top of it and another underneath in the palm so that the hand is open and straight, then wrap everything around the hand tightly and secure the connection between the fingers.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the bone-breaker comes to any of us on the side, if it is the dislocated one, then set it even as it should be.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	And hold it with the palm of your hand, and if you see fit, place a small straight splint to raise the bone-breaker, and do not move it;
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	And if the bone-breaker is on another side, like in the index finger or one of the others, then set it even and tie it with the healthy hand that follows;
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	Or you can bind them all together holding them still, or place a splint on top, as for dislocations.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	And be careful in resetting and disposing of hot abscesses, and treat those who come to it, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Fracture of the thighbone
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The thighbone is often broken, and it is clearly visible when it turns forward and backward;
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	And the reset is this: tie one bandage above the bone-break, and another below.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the patient lies on their face, then each servant extends his rope to his side equally.
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	and this is when the break is within the bone
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the dislocation is near the root of the thigh, then one of the ligaments should be towards the little finger, and the other ligament under the dislocation.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And also if it is near the knee, then let the rope be by the knee, and let the extension be below.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	then the doctor places the bone evenly with both hands, until it is according to its natural shape, and then applies the splint, and the bandage, if no abscess comes out.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if there is a hot abscess, let it cool down before returning to your work and your treatment
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The bandage is made in this manner.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	You must wrap the break with two or three layers of hard doubled bandage, and tie up any excess, then turn the leg so that the heel comes to the root of the thigh, and insert a long string between the hip and the leg, below the knee, and bring the ends of the string upwards.
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then wrap the bandage around the leg and hip, then place the splints on both sides, and place one splint on the bone of the leg;
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then fill the empty space between the leg and hip with soft cloth to create even tension, then begin tying firmly three or four times over the splints.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as you go higher up on the splints, tie less tightly;
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then pass the thread you've placed between the leg and hip around both hips twice, tying three splints that are above them, then return to the bottom of the thread so that it reaches near the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	And tie it tight enough that it does not move from its place, then leave it thus so that no abscess or swelling or similar thing comes.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if any such thing happens, untie it and treat what has come about as we have said many times before.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	And if there are sharp edges of bone protruding, they must be filed down if possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	If this cannot be done, then one must split the joint open and draw fire.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	And treat it as we have said until he is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	Sometimes the thighbone breaks in this way when splints are applied, as in the shoulder or arm;
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	Nevertheless, the patient does not limp with such restoration.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en .l. jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And know that the thighbone is healed in about one month or a little less or more, depending on the variety of temperaments.
de la ruelle dou genoil	Ligamentous injury of the knee
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	Know that in the joint of the knee there is little fracture, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, then it is no more than a crack or hole, and this happens to every wound, and without wound, which everyone feels.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is this: one should place what is around it evenly on its two sides until it is assembled and can move;
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	then put the splint in place, and if necessary use a round splint, and secure it appropriately; then review all the arrangements that we have mentioned for other fractures, such as cauterizing an abscess or similar treatments;
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	So apply to each injury what is necessary until he is healed.
de la brisure de la jambe	Fractures of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that the leg has two bones, one of which is correctly called 'mustelz', and the other 'foscile';
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And likewise breaking happens equally when it comes to the arm, and for that reason restoration is also equal to that of the arm, and the work is all one. And if both bones are broken together, then the limb turns in every direction.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the fibula is broken, turn it forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the big bone is broken, great pain is felt, and it is clearly visible;
et torne desoz.	and it turns underneath.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Therefore arrange for extension, place it evenly, and tie the splints evenly;
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	But nonetheless, if the fracture is ugly with many pieces, the extension should be less and lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	And fasten it according to your skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your work, then take two smooth planks of wood that straddle the leg on both sides, and are as long as the leg from the knee downwards;
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	then wrap it in two places with bandages above and below, tie it in the middle as well, and thus the leg will not bend to the right or left, which is good;
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And some apply hot poultices of the long bones of the leg; if it is wood, they place the leg to prevent movement, and this is properly done in fractures where there is an open wound.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	And move each day the leg to see if there is any heat or other complication.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound heals completely.
de la brisure des os dou piet	"Of the fracture of the bones of the foot"
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	To the ankle there is no fracture,
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there is a bone fracture in the foot, and you see these bones protruding over one another, place the patient's foot on the ground as if they were about to walk, then place your foot upon theirs where the bones are sticking out, and press down until they return to their proper places.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then apply the splint and bandages, place a small board with two legs underneath the foot's stomach, then bind the foot securely, and after wrapping it in cloths, use other necessary items.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	"And when three or four days have passed, undo the bandages, for you will find the bones aligned, whether they were broken or dislocated."
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if any of the toes are broken, restore them as we have said for the fingers of the hand.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place on either broken piece a splint according to the length of the bone, and let it be a bit wider; then place underneath the foot the aforementioned table, and hold it firmly.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are two or three, or more broken pieces, then place on each a splint according to its size, wrapped in one linen cloth, and hold the table firmly underneath the foot.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And let it be, while standing on top of the table, that the sole of the foot touches it well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And you should not forget the other things that I have mentioned for other fractures, as we have said;
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	And treat each case according to what is necessary.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	"Regarding the fracture of the wrist bone"
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bone of a woman's thigh is broken, make her sit wide-legged; then lean her towards the back part, and let her be held from behind;
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the space between her thighs with cotton, also adding as much as one stone's weight;
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then push down the woman, and raise the back little by little, until suddenly the dislocation jumps back in place, and the bone returns with its socket.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she wishes to urinate, remove the dislocation, and once she has urinated, reset it, and do this for about seven days.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If the dislocation is restored, then take a sheep's bladder, attach a tube to its opening, and insert the entire bladder into the joint.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow firmly into the tube until the bladder expands inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The dislocation will then be reset.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then fill it with cotton and leave it like this for a few days until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the bone of the wrist in either men or women is broken, restore it as we have described for the thighbone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	These nearby breaks are not hidden from those who apply their study and practice, and understand my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	Because fracture indicates, in many cases, the direct path to restoration:
enten le donques.	Then take heed.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the leg, when it is broken, take a goose feather and insert the leg into it
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	then wrap bandages around it, and leave it for three days or so, and it will soon be healed
de brisure avec plaie	"Regarding fractures with wounds"
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	He who has a fracture with wound, especially if it is large, such as the bone of the thigh or shoulder or similar, should have his wound cleaned immediately, so that the stitches we have mentioned may testify to this.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, then apply a dressing of vitriol, if you have none other, and then begin to reset the fracture in the same hour or on the same day, unless some obstacle arises.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if some obstacle arises, then leave the reduction until a new day, until the inflammation is subdued, and do not touch it on the third or fourth day, lest you bring on an evil complication.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone appears above the exposed heart, it is necessary that you place it at ease quickly with your hands, with slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extension does not fit to put it evenly in your hands, then use this tool made of iron, which is seven or eight inches long, and its width is according to the quantity of the wound
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and therefore it is necessary for the physician to prepare three or four, depending on what he needs in each case of fracture
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and it should be round and somewhat thick so that it does not bend under pressure on the limb during your operation, and it should be pointed at the front and thick in the middle toward the front, like this
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called 'palainche', therefore the curved head must be placed on the visible top of the bone
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	And push back all at once until it returns, and they are even one against the other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the break is subtle and tools cannot grip the bone well, then you must cut off the head of the bone until tools can grasp it.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot bring back the bone as we have said, then cut off one of its ends with an appropriate instrument, such as a scalpel or saw, with all your strength;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	Then scrape what remains on the bone with sharpness and fine shavings.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset but the patient still feels great pain afterward, know that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	If you do so much that it is in its place, then wet a cloth in black sternutatory wine, and use it properly if it is inflamed;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not put on the wound any cerate or other thing that has oil in it, lest decay and corruption come.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	Then apply dressings when you have restored the bone, leave the wound uncovered, and cut away the surrounding skin according to the size of the wound, and make sure that the wound is not constricted by the fracture.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	And many foolish doctors have done this and caused harm, death or corruption to the patient on several occasions;
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	And let the binding be softer and gentler than other fractures.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is bad or large, and you doubt that some harm may come of it, as we have said, and you find pain in that place, then do not apply plaster.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	But wrap around it instead, using hard cloths, and tie them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after two or three days that the wound is healing, then remove what you had put on previously and apply healing ointment to it, such as tetraformacon ointment and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And it is necessary that you dress the limb twice a day, in the morning and evening, until it is sound and healed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary that the limb be prepared in such a way that the bowels can pass downward easily.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if many days pass and it still cannot heal but the bowels become obstructed again, know that there are small bone fragments causing this pain. Therefore, you must open the wound with a tent, and remove all these unwanted fragments that cause the pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula appears in the place, or another type of corruption, then you must treat it according to what is said in this chapter before.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and lies open on the limb, as in the case of the thighbone or shoulder bone, and other similar large bones, do not pull it out, for many times death ensues, but let it be until it rots.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	Perhaps it will fall off by itself after 20 or 30 days, then dress the wound if you can.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	And if you cannot, then leave it alone.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	And of fractures that come upon the union
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often inquire about the health of the fracture afterwards, especially when it is near the joint, and it is unpleasant to see the deformity of the limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	And by chance, the limb may not be able to perform its natural tasks.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Therefore, take care if the bone is fresh:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If you apply astringent medicines, such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, and sarcocolle, acacia, and similar ones; then take some of these things, or all together, and mix them with astringent wine or with egg white or with honey;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	And put it on the bone in bandages, bind it well, and do not untie it for many days;
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	Then remove it, and begin another one, until the dislocation is healed.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	'Or you can bind it onto a well-made wooden board;'
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	'For the property of wood is that it draws out all swellings from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	And if the dislocation has already turned into hardness like stone, and it is necessary to remove it, then cut on top of it, and remove the excess;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	When you have any razor sharpener, make sure it is properly removed, and clean it thoroughly until it is healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	Of the limb that is weak after the healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When a bone fracture has healed, but afterwards the limb remains weak and frail, this happens for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	One reason is that it was bound too tightly, and not bound as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bandages, preventing the limb from receiving proper nourishment;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to excessive swelling;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or due to moving it too much, not at the appropriate time.
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because there is little blood in its body, making it weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	The treatment for this is to make the patient eat well and exercise their body so that their blood supply increases within them;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and apply baths, provide them with joy and pleasure.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	Then apply pitch to the limb so that it attracts abundant nourishment, and frequently wash it with warm water until proper nourishment reaches the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	And returns to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	Of the limb that is crooked after healing
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the broken bone is apparent, although its natural function remains
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	but do not believe those foolish ones who say that one must break the limb again entirely, and many foolish physicians have done this in our land
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and such practices are blamed, causing great harm, and sometimes death
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	although, if the joints and muscles are fresh, they should be washed with warm water, or softened with herbs cooked, such as fig leaves, roots, and melilot, and similar things
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and apply a softening poultice, such as well-made diachylon, and take the mucilage of figs, and mix it with goose grease or sesame oil, and make a poultice
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or take fat figs, grind them with fennel seed, and similar medications that soften the union
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes the dislocation is removed by rubbing continuously and for a long time with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And arrange gentle movement of the limb each hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the twisted parts are withered and hardened like stone, it is necessary to remove them with iron, cutting gently up to the bone with a fine incision.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and apply care and diligence in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	"Here begins the book of dislocations."
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	"Dislocations occur when a joint moves out of its proper place, preventing it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing great pain and injury to the patient."
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	"If dislocation occurs in anyone, it must be immediately reduced without delay."
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	But if one delays, the area swells, and perhaps it will not be set back in place properly;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	Therefore, one should not move it until it is no longer swollen:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	often brings about spasms and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	However, when this happens, apply a poultice to the patient, then leave it alone until the swelling is relieved;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	then rise the limb with hot water and oil, then gently reset it, and treat each limb as they come back into their proper place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	"And I have arranged the chapters on dislocations from head to foot."
des mandibules	"of the jawbone(s)"
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	It can happen that the lower jaws are dislocated inward, and the dislocation of both is of two kinds:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	either they are a little displaced from their place, or somewhat softened;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	If they are completely dislocated and hang toward the chest, saliva flows from the mouth so that it cannot be held back, nor can the mouth be closed, and the tongue becomes entangled with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	"If the dislocation is slight, it returns on its own through various manipulations."
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is complete and accomplished, then you must reset it quickly, and do not delay;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and do it in such a way that the assistant holds the patient's head and the surgeon puts his little finger of one hand into the root of the jawbone dislocation inside the mouth if the dislocation is on both sides;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and let the other two fingers of the same hand be spread apart to press evenly.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	Tell the patient to soften his jaw and move it in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	"And the doctor places it back into its proper place until it returns."
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if resetting is difficult, especially if both jaws are dislocated together, then warm water and oil should be applied until they can be easily reset.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not delay the resetting, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are reset evenly, and the patient's mouth closes well without softening, then place moistened cloths made from wax and rose oil on it, then tie it lightly with soft linen.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	And let the patient lie on their back, with their head between two pillows so they do not move to the right or left, nor attempt to chew, but take only light food until the pains are relieved and the jaws are numb.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	Then let them chew what they want easily, and do not exert themselves to open their mouth while eating or drinking until the jaws are completely numb and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	"And if the two jawbones cannot be properly reduced within an hour and are not returned to their proper place, then fever and chills will ensue, sometimes with diarrhea, and occasionally with vomiting of bile."
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, then know that it is a lost cause;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many die within nine days upon whom it occurs.
de la forcelle	"of dislocation of the jawbone at the angle"
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	"The angle [of the jaw] cannot be dislocated towards the cheek from within and from below the chin, but sometimes it can be dislocated backwards, which is easily felt."
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the treatment is that the patient lies often on their back and extends their arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	And then press firmly at its place with your hand, and it will return;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	Then put on the bandage and wrap it tightly.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	And the shoulder blade that is towards the back cannot dislocate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	If not, and if it dislocation again, reset it into its place as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then put on the bandage and wrap it tightly, and instruct the patient to rest until they are healed;
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And likewise is reset the shoulder blade when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	"of dislocation of the shoulder blade"
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the shoulder dislocates in only three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	One way is that it dislocation at the part of the socket below;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	And the second way is at the part of the breastbone;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	And sometimes it dislocates above, but this happens rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	And the shoulder does not dislocation behind, nor inward for the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	And many times it dislocates downwards towards the buttock, especially in those who are fatty, for it happens suddenly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	For those who have enough flesh, it hardly jumps or goes back in place.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	"Sometimes, however, some men suffer a blow or a fracture and the shoulder becomes inflamed with heat, causing them to believe that it has been dislocated."
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	It is therefore necessary that you examine it until you are certain;
et adonques encomence la cure.	And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	It is known that dislocations are when they are downwards towards the buttock, and there is a difference between the sick shoulder and the healthy one, which you will find clearly evident between them.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	And you will find a hollow at the top of the shoulder, and when touching below the buttock, you will feel the top of the shoulder like an egg.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	The patient cannot bring their hand to their neck nor move it in any way.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	And likewise, if it is dislocated upwards, it is not concealed because you will find it clearly by touching.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	Only this kind of dislocation can be reduced when it is recent or if the child is sick.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the manner is such that the servant lifts the hand of the patient upwards, then places his thumbs underneath the elbow, and forcibly lifts the joint upwards to its place;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	And the servant raises the hand and extends it upward, then places it underneath;
si venra hastanment.	If it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said within several days afterwards, then the patient must be bathed in warm water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	And the servant should apply moistening and soothing ointments, such as a decoction of mallow, fenugreek, and melilot in water, and it should be applied;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then the patient should be supported on his back, and underneath the elbow a pillow of even cloth should be placed, neither too soft nor too hard; then the physician places his heel on the pillow and gently lifts the shoulder joint, pulling the hand of the patient;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	And another servant should hold the head of the patient so that it does not move downwards;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	This shoulder returns suddenly, if you see it, reset it according to this method:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	And have someone larger than the patient present.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	Let him stand upright facing the side, place his shoulder beneath the arm of the patient, and lift the arm upward so that the patient hangs by it.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	And another helper pulls down the patient's hand towards the stomach.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too light, hang some heavy object with him, and the dislocation will return.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it can also be reset in this other way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And take a long stick and plant it in the ground so that its top is level with the elbow joint, neither too thick nor too thin;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	Then place the patient on top of it, but ensure there are soft cloths underneath, and have the patient stand along the length of the stick;
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Then extend the patient's arm downwards on the other side and quickly reset the shoulder joint.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	And if it does not return despite all these things we have mentioned, then perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	Take a firebrand of two spans long and four fingers wide, which has a round head to easily enter deeply under the armpit, according to this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	then tie onto the head of the prepared wood a cloth so that the wood does not burn the patient; then place it under the armpit of the patient
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extend the patient's arm over the wood lengthwise, and tie the shoulder onto the wood, then place the arm on one end of a wide plank, with the hand extended downwards, and let the body hang freely on the other side
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint will now be ready.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is in, however it may be, then place under the armpit a wisp of wool; then put on the emplaster made with flour powder, with incense and egg yolk all around the shoulder, then wrap it tightly under the armpit, and twist the bandage onto the plaster, and bind the hand to its collar, and let the hand remain like this.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And he should fast little, so that the limb may rest comfortably, for it will heal more quickly
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then start eating again after five or seven days, and move the limb
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is firm and not softened, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint has been forced out of place due to moisture that has come there, or for some other reason, then you must administer cauteries with three openings, as it is described in the chapter on cauteries.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this, but after seven days the dislocation remains and he cannot raise his arm upwards, then know that the nerves at the head of the shoulder are cut or stretched or weakened
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	And know that the joint will never again be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that is towards the hip, and the breasts, or behind, if it occurs by impulse and extension of hands, one should apply another bandage.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after the healing there comes pain in the member and slowness of movement, then the patient should often apply hot compresses until that pain is alleviated and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	About dislocation of the elbow
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the shoulder joint is dislocated by force, and returns by force;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	and if it has been dislocated in all directions, especially front and back, the dislocation is not hidden, as one can see and feel it well;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And it becomes dislocated according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick shoulder with the healthy one, so you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is dislocated and cannot bend the arm or touch the shoulder completely
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you must reset it before an abscess appears there, for if an abscess appears there, it would be difficult to reset;
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and perhaps it cannot be completely reset, especially when it is behind.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	So this dislocation is worse than others and causes great pain, and sometimes death occurs there.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And its restoration is when it can be brought back such that you extend your hand with both of yours;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And spread his arms wide, and with your hands grasp the elbow around, above and below, pushing the joint into place at the base of the thumb or palm until it returns to its proper position;
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is in front, then it returns when he folds his hand towards his hand and presses the elbow that is dislocated against the root of the palm.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to its place, then administer strong traction;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and have two ministers extend the arm, and two ministers hold it so that it does not move during the extension;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then twist the arm in both directions, then after you have wrapped a long and wide doubled cloth around it;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the surgeon has placed the joint in his hand, then anoint it with some oil to soften the joint, then forcefully push the joint until it returns;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, then put on a dry compress with egg yolk, press it firmly, and bind the arm around the patient's neck, leaving it there for some days before removing it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, then loosen it with a bandage.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you see that the joint is not set properly, then recommence the placement and loosen it with a bandage, and leave it thus for several days until it is firmly in place.
puis le deslie.	Then remove the bandage.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if it feels sore after resetting the joint and moves, then bathe and gently rub it and press until it feels soothed.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Or place a grease made of mutton fat on the joint, then leave it for one day and one night, then remove it, and let it enter into a bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when it begins to sweat, gently rub the joint, then replace the grease, and then enter the bath.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this twice or three times until it is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see that it is still not well, then place moist fenugreek flour warmed with butter on it and bind it tightly.
si revenra a sa disposition.	If it returns to its position
li dislocation de la main	hand dislocations
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The dislocated joint of the hand returns, and its return is light, more so than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it must be quickly reset to its place in the same wound where it was dislocated, before the area becomes inflamed or an abscess forms.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the resetting is done thus: you place the injured hand on a table, and extend it with the help of assistants. The physician then places their palm flat against the front of the joint, pushing until it returns to its proper position.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you must ensure that it is properly in place;
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then the patient places the back of their hand on a table at full extension and during the reset.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is in the back of the hand, then the patient places their backhand on the table, and the physician places his hand over its joint surface.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, then apply soothing plasters to alleviate any heat or swelling, and leave them on without restarting the process.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, nor can you put it back into place after several days, then the joint remains dislocated.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	Nor does any harm come to the patient from this, except that his hand becomes weakened and he cannot grasp anything until
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then you know that the nerves are cut or the arteries
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	If there is no other injury except pulling with forceps near the case, and sometimes nothing else helps.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	"And when the hand is in place, put on the splint that we have mentioned, then bind it and leave it for five days, then untie it and let it remain so."
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if he cannot move it well, and there is any stiffness, then apply warm water and rub until it is smooth."
de la dislocation des dois de la main	"Regarding the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Sometimes both hands are dislocated on either side, sometimes at the back of the palm or the front
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Then grasp both hands and push the dislocation back into place as far as it goes; then hold the top of the hand steady and tilt it towards the side where it was dislocated
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and let it rest for 2 days, and then set it straight on the third day
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and wrap it up as we have said, and on the fourth day remove the dressing, wash it, and move it gently while keeping it wrapped.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this often, until it is tight, and also do so if the shoulder blade dislocates at the stomach of the hand; and do it in the same way you did before, until it is in place.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	And likewise do when it is dislocated elsewhere.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	"Regarding the dislocation of the heel bone of the back"
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	"When the heel bone of the foot or leg is dislocated, or when there are multiple dislocations, there is no treatment for this, as the damage is already done."
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the sign of this is that the joints move suddenly without intention and cannot be held in place, and many times some member, such as both thighs or both arms, becomes paralyzed.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the backbone moves into four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	That which moves at the rear is called 'gilbositez':
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The treatment for this is to watch if the gilbositez has come from infancy:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no hope of cure or healing.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or blows or similar things, the ancient doctors proposed various treatments with grand words, but they did not have great benefit in all cases;
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have summarized it according to my intention and formed tools in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the swelling that occurs in the chest before, none has health;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also that which comes directly to both sides, and one cannot cure it outside except that which comes to the back, as I say.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And it is necessary for the patient to be laid on their face in one even place, and have something underneath them so they do not bruise.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then stick one ember at the head firmly into the ground, and another at the feet, and tie a band across the patient's buttocks, and another at the hips, knees, and ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	And two attendants hold the bands, one at the head and the other at the feet, between the two embers;
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	And let them be held firmly together, the ember as we have said, and the physician place their palms strongly on the spine until it returns.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return with this cure, then take a board three spans long and lay it under the patient's back, with the patient on their side, and put the end of the board under the backbone, then place the middle of the board on the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	And let the master put his feet on the other end of the table, and press firmly until it returns to its place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	And if you see that, do it to the one that turns towards the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And you should place two stakes at the top of the patient's arm and two others towards their feet, with a handspan distance between each stake.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	And there should be one hole in each stake where the dislocation occurs, and the stakes should be firmly fixed into the ground so that they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And between each of the two stakes should be one turning stake, upon which the rope will turn, and there should be two small stakes a handspan long on either side to help rotate the dislocation.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	And then tie the rope that is among the stakes to the turning stake towards the top, and the other rope towards the feet at the other turning stake. Each of the assistants should rotate their turning stake with all the ropes, and the master should keep the tension even as we have described.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is equal, then place a drying plaster with plenty of egg, and then the dressings, and then the hot iron of a tablet of three ounces long, that it may touch the place of the gibbosity and the part of the healthy spine, then tie it with a linen thread, as we have said, and let the patient use subtle nourishment until he is healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	And if anything prevents recovery at the end of healing, then it is necessary to administer softening and soothing medications with the hot iron that we have mentioned before.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	And sometimes one administers a piece of lead, and sometimes the appearance comes in the back spine of the back, and it is thought that this is dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	And this is the bone that appears, therefore one must not presume to do so:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	For it might bring death upon him.
des dislocations de la hainche	"Dislocations of the hip joint"
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that in the joints of the hip and the joints of the shoulder there comes forth only dislocation, unlike other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	And the joint of the hip is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	within and without, before and behind;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	And further inward, otherwise dislocated in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation inward is that when one joins the sick leg with the healthy one, it is longer, and the sick knee opens wider than the healthy one, and the sick person cannot bend their knee towards the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and the place that is near it is swollen with a hot abscess because the head of the thigh goes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	"And the sign of external hip dislocation is that these accidents are opposite to those mentioned earlier."
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the sign of that which happens in front is that one can hardly straighten their leg to its full extent;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	Nevertheless, they cannot bend their knee without pain, and if one tries to make them walk, they cannot go forward, and they retain their urine, and the ankle swells, and when they walk, they limp on their heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	"And the sign of posterior hip dislocation is that the knee cannot be extended or bent, and the leg appears shorter than the other one. The ankle is relaxed, and the thighbone is located below the ribs."
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The treatment of this kind of dislocation is that if the dislocation is ancient and it remains in its place, there is no treatment for it;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	And there should be no presumption in this.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in the case where the dislocation is fresh, and there are four types of dislocation, quickly reset the joint, extend it inward and outward, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	Perhaps it will return, and no other treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, then you must prepare a strong assistant and firmly extend the leg with both hands or have one foot tied above the knee
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and another assistant extends their hand in such a way that they place their hands beneath the buttocks, then pulls strongly with one swift movement towards the hip
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And another holds onto the end of the rope.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And they all pull upwards and downwards simultaneously until the patient is lifted off the ground all at once and hangs suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This manner of extension is common for four members, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, that is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then treat it in a similar manner.
