Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the hip area, place the patient on their healthy side, then put the rope on the root of the hip and the location below the angle, then pull the rope upwards towards the angle and towards the thigh
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then take another helper's arms, and embrace the large bone of the sick hip, and extend it forcefully:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	and it will now return to its place.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	And this manner of dislocation is easier than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot fix it in the manner we have described, then you must tie the two feet of the patient together with a soft strong bandage on both heels and knees, and let the sick leg extend two fingers more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then hang it from the top of a post, and have two long arms above the ground
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then instruct one helper to embrace the top of the hip, and have another helper hanging with the patient, who forcefully embraces the hip, for the joint will now return quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation has returned, have the patient lie down as we described for those with gout, and carefully remove the bandage from the sick leg and also from the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two brands: one at the head and another at the feet; then insert one brand between the thighs of the patient in this shape;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And have moistened cloths ready around it so that the patient does not burn; then extend each assistant towards him, and the physician set his hand equal to the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, that's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place a stone on it, and press it as we have said in the chapter on gibbosity (kyphosis), with the patient lying on the sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is before (visible), it is necessary to extend the affected leg quickly; as I have said
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and the physician place his pain (palm) on top of the sick joint; then press with the other hand, and stretch down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is behind, then it is not necessary to extend the sick leg downwards or lift it up; rather, it must be as if the hip were dislocated backwards, as we have said regarding childbirth on both hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and lie him on his face; and stretch out the linen as we have said earlier, and everyone must press on the joint together.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	And it will be ready when the patient extends their legs, and they are even.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then join the thighs together, place the splint, and bind it with a bandage so that the hip does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And let it rest for three or four days, then untie it and place the splint on top;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, bind them as before, and leave them for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then untie it, and let him walk gently until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee joint can be dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, inside and out, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is this: tell the patient to bend their leg towards their thigh, and if it does not articulate with their thigh, know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the reduction of all three kinds is this: have the patient sit up straight, extend their leg if possible, and place your back against their face, and place their foot on yours;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take his knee in your palms, and draw it between your thighs, then strongly bend both sides of the knee.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another assistant extends his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign that it is well put back is when he can easily move his leg at the hip.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the plaster on top, and bind the leg to the thigh, tying them together tightly for three or four days, then untie it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not let the patient move until the member is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not yet straight, then extend it strongly, as we have said in the treatment of the thigh, until it is straight.
de la dislocation dou talon	Dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	"The heel is sometimes twisted and sometimes completely dislocated, both inward and outward."
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign that it is well put back is when the ankle is swollen and sticks out on the side where it was dislocated
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reduction should be easy, and one can easily extend the arm with both hands when it is only slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is completely dislocated, you should make the patient sit upright, and one assistant should pull him forward by the leg above the ankle
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then draw the foot towards you with your right hand, then with your left hand twice, then stretch it out upwards, and gently place the foot up high.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	And do this twice, as we have said, while pushing and pulling the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it stays in place, that's good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, then start again, for it will dislocate again.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it still cannot stay in place, then have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly plant a pole in the earth between their thighs, and tie straps around so as not to hurt the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then two ministers grasp the thigh, while another extends the foot towards them or lies down on it, so that they can tie it at the ankle joint.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then each minister stretches out equally, and let the pole be between the patient's thighs to hold them down when stretching out.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then the physician gently places his hands on the dislocation and another minister grasps the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will quickly return to its place.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it reaches its peak, then place the plaster and bandages on it, press firmly, tie the foot to the leg, and keep watch over the nerves that are above the ankle behind, so that the bindings are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the bindings get loose, then press firmly;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then untie it on the third or fourth day, and prohibit the patient from walking for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if he walks before that time, there is no certainty that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if inflammation comes afterwards, then you must calm it as we have said elsewhere until it is healed."
des dois	about the elbows
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	"When the elbows are dislocated, they should be gently reduced without force, and this is an easy thing to do."
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any knot of the back of the foot, then have the patient sit on a flat surface or on a table entirely straight, and place your foot on what opens up from these joints, then press firmly with your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	Then when it is even and nothing opens up, place two-footed table under the sole of the foot, then press firmly, leave for three days, then untie.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	About wounds and dislocations at the same time
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When an injury comes with the dislocation and one wants to reset it, many times the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	Do not be presumptuous in treatment if you are not wise in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate, merciful, and careful, not hasty.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	And at the beginning of treating hot inflammation, use soothing remedies, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then reset the limb to its place before the inflammation becomes hot.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and once the limb is in place, then apply soothing remedies for hot inflammation and treat the wound with drying ointments as necessary;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is also a fracture along with the dislocation and small bones dislocated, set them, and do what we have said for simple bone fractures;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard yourself from entering a path of fear, as I have said, for it is against your movement according to your Creator, and for the knowledge of your arms and body.
